Content of Exchange of Letters Between Britain, France, and Belgium 56

(Paris) In accordance with the draft agreement established at the Locarno Conference, the British government will send letters to France and Belgium to guarantee the security of each country. The letter sent to France is divided into two parts:

The first part is to stipulate the meaning and scope of the talks between the general staffs of Britain, France, and Belgium, and French Ambassador to Britain, Corbin, has replied that he will comply.

The second part is a statement that the British government should take various measures to guarantee the security of France, which was issued on April 1st and only announced today. The content is summarized as follows:

British First Letter

It roughly states, "The general staffs of Britain, France, and Belgium may immediately begin contact in accordance with Article 3 of the Locarno Agreement draft, but this contact may not give rise to any political obligations, nor should it accept any restrictions on the defense organizations of the countries concerned. It is believed that your government must have the same view, and your Excellency the Ambassador is requested to make a statement. As for the location of the talks between the general staffs of the three countries, this Minister also proposes that it be held in London."

French Reply

It roughly states, "Having received your letter stating that the general staffs of Britain, France, and Belgium may immediately begin contact in accordance with the Locarno Agreement draft, but this contact may not give rise to any political obligations, nor should the military organizations of the countries concerned accept any restrictions. We hereby reply to express our agreement. As for the fact that the talks between the general staffs of the three countries are scheduled to be held in London, we can also agree."

British Second Letter

It provides various guarantees, roughly stating that if the current mediation efforts fail, the British government should immediately take the following measures:

(A) Immediately consider appropriate means with France and Belgium to deal with the situation at that time.

(B) Immediately come forward to assist France in accordance with the provisions of the Locarno Treaty and the methods jointly decided by the countries concerned.

(C) If France is invaded without provocation, the British government should immediately consult with France and take all practical measures to protect French security, but the French government must also assume the same obligations to Britain.

(D) The general staffs of the countries concerned should begin or continue contact in order to achieve the above-mentioned objectives.

(E) Britain should work together with France to request the Executive Yuan of the League of Nations to put forward proposals so that peace can be maintained and the rule of international law can be respected.

French Reply

It roughly states, "Having received your letter, we hereby declare our agreement in the name of the government."

Japanese Navy to Expand Air Power 57

Six Major Bases to Be Established Nationwide; Completion Expected by October This Year

(Tokyo) In order to expand naval air power, the Ministry of the Navy plans to establish six major air bases in Kanazawa, Ominato, Kanoya, Jinhae, Kisarazu, and Maizuru. Exchange of Letters Between the Three Countries Announced Yesterday; If Mediation Efforts Fail, Britain Guarantees the Security of France and Belgium; The General Staffs of the Three Countries Will Meet in London; Britain Retains Political Avoidance of New Obligations 58

(London) British Foreign Secretary Eden handed letters from the British government to the ambassadors of France and Belgium at the Foreign Office last night. The letters stated that if mediation fails, Britain is willing to guarantee the security of France and Belgium to resist unwarranted aggression. Eden also gave another letter, which reportedly mentioned that the scope of the talks between the general staffs of France and Britain should be limited to politics. In addition, the mutual obligations stipulated in the first letter will only take effect after the governments of Britain, France, and Belgium decide that mediation has failed. Eden will announce his views on the German government's reply in the House of Commons today. Eden met with German Special Envoy Ribbentrop yesterday. Ribbentrop also held a meeting with Vansittart, the permanent head of the Foreign Office. It is reported that Ribbentrop will stay in London for several days. (3rd Reuters Dispatch)

(London) Based on the draft agreement established at the Locarno Conference on March 19, the British government will send letters to France and Belgium to guarantee the security of each country. Foreign Secretary Eden handed over these letters to French Ambassador Corbin and Belgian Ambassador Machian at 6:15 PM this afternoon. In addition, another letter stating that the general staffs of Britain, France, and Belgium should immediately begin contact in accordance with Article 3 of the Locarno Agreement draft was also delivered at the same time. (Note: Article 3 of the draft agreement states that during the transition period, in order to implement the mutual assistance provisions of the Locarno Treaty, the general staffs of the countries concerned should hold talks to maintain the effectiveness of the treaty until a new treaty is established to replace the original Locarno Treaty.) The government has now decided to compile these letters and various documents related to the talks between the general staffs of the three countries into a White Paper and submit it to the House of Commons tomorrow. (2nd Havas Dispatch)

(Paris) A spokesman for the Ministry of Foreign Affairs recently announced that the letter that the British government should put forward to guarantee the security of France and Belgium in accordance with the Locarno draft agreement has been sent by British Foreign Secretary Eden to French Ambassador to Britain Corbin. The content of this letter is very similar to the original wording of the draft agreement. In addition, another letter was also sent at the same time as the previous letter, which defines the meaning and scope of the talks that should be held between the general staffs of Britain, France, and Belgium. In short, (that is, the participating countries cannot give rise to any new political obligations, and the military organizations of the countries concerned are also not affected by this (referring to Britain's unwillingness to take any preparatory measures in national defense, such as adopting conscription)). After receiving the letter from the British government, Ambassador Corbin to Britain submitted two reply letters to British Foreign Secretary Eden. The first letter stated that the British letter had been received and that the wording of the letter was copied to show that the security guarantee has now become a relative mutual assistance system. The second letter on the meaning and scope of the talks between the general staffs of the three countries also follows the wording of the British letter. However, the above exchange of letters did not specify the date for the talks between the general staffs. (2nd Havas Dispatch)

British Foreign Secretary Explains the Diplomatic Situation to the House of Commons; Will Do His Best to Promote Peace Negotiations 59

(London) British Foreign Secretary Eden mentioned the German reply in the House of Commons today, saying that the events of the past few days are divided into two categories: one is related to the German government's letter stating the new European peace plan, and the other is related to the exchange of documents between the governments of Britain, France, and Belgium involving the White Paper of March 19. On April 1, German Special Envoy Ribbentrop went to the Foreign Office to deliver the German reply. Yesterday, he told Ribbentrop that the British government only had time for a preliminary study of Germany's recent proposals and will continue to study them because it believes they are very important and should be carefully reviewed. He also told him that Britain's goal is to make negotiations progress so as to promote a final solution, and Britain will do its best to achieve this goal. Please convey this to Hitler. However, Germany has not yet adopted the British government's idea for an interim period.

The British Foreign Secretary then declared to the House of Commons that the future talks between the general staffs of Britain, France, and Belgium will not increase Britain's political obligations. These talks only involve the interim period when negotiations are not in progress and are purely technical in nature. The British government has explained to the governments of France and Belgium that the letter sent to France and Belgium yesterday, which re-stated Britain's obligation to uphold the Locarno Treaty, does not contain the intention of Britain recognizing that reconciliation has failed. The talks between the general staffs will begin in London, and the date has not yet been determined, but they will be held as soon as the necessary arrangements have been made. The main purpose of Britain's decision to hold talks between the general staffs is only to help restore trust. The British government believes that these talks will not hinder the solution. In answering Lloyd George's question, the British Foreign Secretary said that military plans will never be implemented unless France or Belgium is attacked without provocation. In answering a question from Conservative Party member Esther, the British Foreign Secretary said that although British overseas autonomous territories are not signatories to the Locarno Treaty, the British government will inform them in detail of the various processes of the negotiations. As for the fact that Italy had written to France and Belgium in the capacity of guarantor of the Locarno Treaty, stating that it was willing to uphold the obligations of the Locarno Treaty, which was the same as that issued by Britain yesterday, he had not heard of it. (3rd Reuters Dispatch)

(London) The House of Commons held a meeting today, and Captain Peter MacDonald, a Conservative Party member, asked the government about the talks that should be held between the general staffs of Britain, France, and Belgium. Prime Minister Baldwin answered them one by one. The Prime Minister also declared that regarding the situation caused by the German memorandum, Foreign Secretary Eden is scheduled to attend the House of Commons at 11:00 AM tomorrow to issue a declaration. The questions and answers between MacDonald and the Prime Minister are excerpted below:

(MacDonald asked) Is Italy going to participate in the talks that should be held between the general staffs of the countries concerned?

(Prime Minister replied) The general staff talks that the British government currently agrees to participate in are those held jointly with the general staffs of France and Belgium. As for the fact that the Italian government is planning to hold the same talks with France and Belgium, the British government has not received any information.

(MacDonald asked) Can these general staff talks be postponed until progress has been made in the negotiations with Germany before they begin?

(Prime Minister replied) The talks that should be held between the general staffs of Britain, France, and Belgium are to discuss the current situation. This has been explained by Foreign Secretary Eden. If negotiations with Germany are to succeed, the trust between the countries concerned must be restored. These general staff talks are an element of restoring trust, so the government cannot agree to the postponement proposal.

(MacDonald asked) Please provide assurances to the House of Commons that these general staff talks must be strictly supervised by the Cabinet, and that the purpose must be limited to defense and must not be developed for war against Germany, as advocated by Louis George, the leader of the opposition Liberal Party.

(Prime Minister replied) I would like to assure you today that the government will supervise these talks effectively and strictly. As for Louis George's claim, it is purely fantasy. (3rd Havas Dispatch)

Eden Asks the German Representative Several Questions 60

(London) When British Foreign Secretary Eden met with German Special Envoy Ribbentrop at the Foreign Office yesterday, he raised several questions, which Ribbentrop noted down one by one. He will probably answer verbally after Easter. The main question is, what does Germany mean by saying that if Germany rejoins the League of Nations, it will demand equal colonial rights within a considerable period of time? Does "considerable period" mean half a year, one year, or longer? Does Germany want to recover all or part of its former colonies? Other questions related to the definition of "troops" in the March 7 memorandum of Hitler, including irregular troops and air forces. Eden also asked about Germany's intention to conclude mutual non-aggression pacts with Lithuania, Czechoslovakia, and Austria, and whether Germany wanted to abandon the Hague International Court of Justice and establish a new international court. (3rd Reuters Dispatch)

(London) German representative Ribbentrop visited Foreign Office official Sir Westaj at noon and held a long talk. Afterwards, Ribbentrop spoke with Führer Hitler on a long-distance telephone for a long time. According to people from the German embassy, ​​Ribbentrop will stay in London for several days and has not yet made a decision. (2nd Havas Dispatch)

(London) Regarding the issue of Germany concluding mutual assistance treaties with neighboring countries, it was recently stated by people close to the German delegation that Germany is only willing to sign such treaties with its western neighbors and is unwilling to conclude them with eastern Austria, Czechoslovakia, Poland, and the Soviet Union. It is said that "the policies of these countries are unstable and hostile to each other, forming a confrontation. If Germany were to conclude mutual assistance treaties with them, it might have to act as an arbitrator between these countries, which Germany does not want." Therefore, according to Germany, it is better to sign a general airspace agreement and include the above-mentioned countries. (2nd Havas Dispatch)

Hitler Declares in Parliament the Abandonment of the Locarno Treaty

German Memorandum: Reactions in Paris 62

Believed to be of a completely negative nature, sufficient to cause the League of Nations itself to fail.

(Paris) French authorities believe that Hitler's reply to the four-power proposal, in the form of a memorandum, is completely negative. They say that the German proposal would lead to the failure of the collective security and mutual assistance system, as well as the League of Nations itself. The signatories of the Locarno Treaty all believe that before beginning negotiations to reorganize European peace, the international laws broken by Germany must at least be partially restored. However, Germany has now rejected almost all of the proposed plans. The German memorandum disregards the International Court of Justice at The Hague and proposes a new arbitration court, without providing detailed explanations. This action is a major blow to the League of Nations. (Reuters, 2nd)

(Paris) The reactions of various circles here to the German reply can be summarized in the following three points: Whether the "Security Pact" proposed in the German reply can be compatible with existing mutual assistance pacts without conflict; The points concerning the restriction of air force actions proposed in the German reply do not seem to be included in the proposed Sky Pact; Germany insists that it can only rejoin the League of Nations if other countries do not intervene in its treaty violations. (National Telegram, 2nd)

Berlin Citizens Cheer as Troops March to the Rhineland, Shouting Slogans of Equality

Therefore, the strategies adopted cannot be the same. Once the defensive fortifications on the Rhine River are completed, Germany will not have to worry about interference from Britain and France, and will have no worries about its western flank. Then, it can develop towards Eastern and Central Europe. This must be prevented. As for France, it still advocates peace as a whole and adheres to the principle of collective security. No matter how the international situation develops in the future, France's actions will be based on this attitude. (Havas, 2nd)

Abyssinian Government Sends Note to League of Nations, Requesting Financial Assistance, and Intensifying Sanctions Against Italy 65

Ethiopia Expresses Doubt Whether Italy's Acceptance of Invitation to Negotiate Peace with the League of Nations is Sincere

(Geneva) The Abyssinian government has made three appeals to the League of Nations: Financial assistance; Removal of obstacles that some member states of the League of Nations are still imposing on the transportation of military equipment to the Abyssinian army; Exerting utmost efforts to intensify the current sanctions against Italy to the fullest extent. (Reuters, 2nd)

(Geneva) The Abyssinian government has sent a note to League of Nations Secretary-General Avenol, requesting that the League of Nations intensify sanctions against Italy and provide financial assistance to Abyssinia. It stated that although Italy has accepted the application of the Committee of Thirteen of the League of Nations Administrative Council and has agreed in principle to begin peace talks, the war continues as before, and the methods of warfare used are extremely brutal. It is hoped that the League of Nations will take prompt action towards the Italian government so that it respects wartime laws. The conclusion states, "It is the important duty of the member states of the League of Nations to make justice prevail over power. The Abyssinian government specifically reiterates this point and hopes that it will not be seen as an extravagant request." (Havas, 2nd)

If the country ceases military action during the negotiation period, then we will believe that it has peaceful intentions." (Havas, 2nd)

(Rome) Although the Italian government has accepted the letter from the chairman of the Committee of Thirteen (the Spanish representative), Madariaga, inviting it to discuss ways to resolve the East African war, the hope of finding a way to end the war quickly under the auspices of the Committee of Thirteen seems very slim. According to political circles here, the plan of the Committee of Five and the proposals agreed upon by Hoare and Laval but abandoned, which were previously regarded as a possible basis for resolving the East African war, are no longer an issue. Regarding the rumor that the Abyssinian Emperor has sent a special envoy to meet with the commander-in-chief of the Italian army, official circles here have denied it. Although it is not widely believed that Mussolini has put forward concrete peace proposals, the French ambassador is now returning to Paris for vacation, and it is generally thought that the ambassador may take this opportunity to inquire about the opinions of his government. (Reuters, 2nd)

Italian Army Approaches Lake Tana, Britain Greatly Disturbed 66

Anti-Italian Sentiment Continues to Reignite, Italy Denies Any Political Motives

(London) The recent victories of the Italian army in Abyssinia, including the capture of Gondar, bringing them closer to the British sphere of influence, have caused concern in Britain. Coupled with the Italian army's brutal methods of warfare, British people, filled with indignation, have seen a resurgence of anti-Italian sentiment. People supporting the League of Nations are now promoting the policy of intensifying sanctions against Italy and have scheduled a large-scale rally on the 9th of this month to call for support. The executive committee of the Federation of Organizations Supporting the League of Nations has also passed a resolution, the core of which is that Italy should immediately cease its war against Abyssinia, and the Committee of Eighteen of the League of Nations should decide on effective sanctions to be imposed on Italy, such as an oil embargo, restrictions on oil shipping, and, if necessary, cutting off transportation between Italy and Abyssinia. (Havas, 3rd)

(Rome) Responsible officials here declared today that although the Lake Tana area is within Britain's sphere of influence, Britain need not worry about the Italian army's advance into locations near the lake, because Prime Minister Mussolini will surely be consistent in word and deed and respect British interests in the area. They denied that the Italian army's occupation of the area had any political motives and that the decision to attack was motivated by taking advantage of Britain's focus on the Rhineland issue, leaving it no time to attend to other matters, to resolve the Italian-Abyssinian dispute by force. Officials declared that their motives were purely military in nature. Today's war report stated that in addition to Gondar, the Italian army has also captured the towns of Massatanki and Raffa'i. Many members of the Abyssinian Emperor's Imperial Guard have surrendered to the Italian army. The Abyssinian Emperor is now retreating rapidly towards Taissy. The Italian air force is now attacking Taissy from both the east and west sides, and the air force and artillery are also very active north of Lake Ashangi. (National Telegram, 2nd)

(Rome) Since occupying the city of Gondar in northern Abyssinia, Italy is now only a few dozen kilometers away from Lake Tana, the source of the Blue Nile. It is rumored that people in the Italian cotton industry have devised a plan to block the lake water to prevent it from flowing into the Blue Nile and its tributaries, thereby harming British cotton planting in British-controlled Egypt and Sudan. This statement has been denied by the semi-official Italian newspaper Il Popolo d'Italia, which called it a fabrication and said that the Italian government has accepted and will continue to abide by the restrictions (as stipulated in the 1925 Anglo-Italian Protocol). Therefore, all British interests currently within Abyssinia will remain intact. The above rumors are just a tactic adopted by some newspapers to confuse the public. "It is regrettable that this kind of conspiracy is occurring at this time." (Havas, 3rd)

Abyssinian Army Concentrates Elite Troops to Defend the Makhani Region, Of Extreme Strategic Importance 67

The Makhani region, south of Abyssinian capital Addis Ababa and Enba Arraschi, controls the vital routes to Taissy and Addis Ababa, and is of extreme strategic importance, making it a place that both armies must fight for. The gain or loss of this road is enough to determine the victory or defeat of the overall situation. Therefore, the Italian military authorities are threatening the Abyssinian army defending this line with the greatest military force, and almost all of the elite troops assigned to defend this line are the Abyssinian side's best troops, including the Imperial Guard personally commanded by the Abyssinian Emperor, in an attempt to make a final stand. The fierceness of the fighting is unprecedented since the start of the war. The Italian army relies on the shelling of field artillery, the bombing of the air force, and the simultaneous advance of armored vehicles and tanks. As for the Abyssinian army, they use stillness to counter movement, focusing on close combat. The great battle has not yet ended. Military authorities here are quickly mobilizing all reserve soldiers in order to support the Abyssinian army on the front lines. (National News Agency, 3rd)

Heavy Casualties on Both Sides in the Battle of Lake Ashangi 68

Asmara. According to news from the Italian military headquarters, a fierce battle took place between the Italian and Abyssinian armies in the Lake Ashangi area in northern Abyssinia on the 31st of last month. As a result, the Italian army won a great victory. In this battle, Italian officers and soldiers suffered approximately 1,200 casualties. The Abyssinian army suffered heavy casualties, and even Minister of Posts and Communications Makos was killed. The Italian air force was extremely active in this battle. The day was foggy, and all aircraft had to fly at low altitude, so 17 aircraft were hit by various types of Abyssinian bullets, four of which were heavily damaged. However, only three air force personnel were injured. After the battle, all aircraft returned to their bases. It seems that the Imperial Guard commanded by the Abyssinian Emperor is concentrated in the Mali an Achangi Mahakchi area northeast of Lake Ashangi. It is possible that the Abyssinian Emperor intends to fight the Italian army again, but some believe that after this heavy blow, the Abyssinian Emperor may decide to sue for peace with the Italian army. (Havas, 3rd)

Addis Ababa. The government recently issued a communique stating that on the 31st of last month, Abyssinian troops in the north attacked the Mai Kiwote Batta area, and four of the seven small fortresses set up by the Italian army were captured by the Abyssinian army. Two hundred Italian white soldiers and one thousand indigenous troops were killed. On the 1st of this month, Abyssinian troops in the north engaged the Italian army again. The Italian army was unable to resist and retreated in defeat, leaving behind 500 corpses, including 36 officers and 200 indigenous soldiers, as well as many machine guns and several cannons. On the Abyssinian side, a total of 887 soldiers were killed and 345 were injured. From this point of view, although the Italian artillery fire was extremely fierce, the Abyssinian army was still able to achieve a great victory. (Havas, 2nd)

Asmara. According to news from the Italian military headquarters, small teams of Abyssinian troops have recently attempted to infiltrate the Italian front lines in Bameikang and Zaifdi in the north, but they have all been repelled by the Italian army and suffered heavy losses. In addition, a large number of Abyssinian deserters have come to the Italian front lines to surrender, most of whom are members of the Abyssinian Emperor's Imperial Guard. (Havas, 3rd)

Foreign Minister Arita's Remarks After Assuming Office: Not Bound by the Three Principles Towards China 72

Emphasis on Removing Obstacles to Economic Development, East Asia Policy Includes Engagement with Britain and the United States, The US Government Expresses Goodwill Towards Arita

(Tokyo) In a statement after assuming office, Foreign Minister Hachiro Arita strongly emphasized the two points of defending against the Red ideology and breaking away from the current state of economic foundation. According to the new Foreign Minister, during the past month, he was stationed in China as ambassador, exchanged opinions with the Chinese leadership, and on the way back home, he detoured through North China, entered "Manchukuo," and repeatedly consulted with Japanese government-appointed organizations. As a result, he is well aware that in implementing the China policy and maintaining close relations between Japan and Manchukuo, the urgent task should be to remove obstacles hindering Japan's trade and economic development through diplomatic efforts, so that Japan's economic diplomacy can have a bright future. To implement this policy, it is necessary to do so with decisive determination. Therefore, in the China policy, there is no need to adhere to the so-called three principles, and national relations should be gradually adjusted using methods appropriate to the situation. Anti-communism between China and Japan is a priority. In the policy towards Russia, the first priority should be to resolve pending issues and strive for the concretion of the inseparable relationship between Japan and Manchukuo. As for the East Asia policy, it should not only be a policy for handling the mutual relations of East Asian countries, but should also include the policies towards Britain and the United States. Under the slogan of unifying diplomacy, he intends to implement what he believes in. (Domei, 3rd)

Washington. There is goodwill here towards the newly appointed Japanese Foreign Minister Arita. Arita once served as the First Secretary of the Japanese Embassy in the United States and is very familiar with the relationship between the United States and the Pacific. Arita will probably continue Hirota's policy, trying to improve trade relations between Japan and the United States, and calmly deal with thorny issues between the two countries. Recent Situation of the Northeastern Volunteer Army 73

Total Number Not Less Than 150,000, Divided into Two Units to Fight the Enemy in Guerrilla Warfare

(Changchun) According to reliable sources, the number of volunteer soldiers has recently increased several times compared to before. Their total number is no less than 150,000. The main base area is around the Chinese Eastern Railway, and the rest are scattered in Hunchun, Panshi, Zhuhe, Mishan, Hulin, Dongning, Ning'an, Muling, Zichuan, Tangyuan, and other places. The organization is divided into two units. One is called the Northeastern Anti-Japanese Allied Army, which is divided into six armies. Its strength is the most powerful, its equipment is completely modernized, and its warfare is based on guerrilla tactics that divide into smaller units. Moreover, it has densely deployed cell organizations in various rural villages, and its intelligence is extremely sensitive. Therefore, although the Japanese and Manchukuo armies have continuously "suppressed" them, they have not been able to harm them in the slightest. The names of the commanders of each army are as follows: Yang Jingyu, commander of the First Army; Wang Detai, commander of the Second Army; Zhao Shangzhi, commander of the Third Army; Li Yanlu, commander of the Fourth Army; Zhou Baozhong, commander of the Fifth Army; Xie Wendong, commander of the Sixth Army. The second is called the Northeastern Volunteer Army, commanded by Commander-in-Chief Wu Yicheng and Deputy Commander Kong Xiancheng. Its combat effectiveness is also very strong, but its equipment is slightly inferior to that of the Anti-Japanese Allied Army. (Hualian Telegram, 3rd)

Face is an important factor in the Far East. If Soviet Russia rejects its invasion, then the Japanese government will feel that for the sake of Japan's prestige, it must support the Kwantung Army. The answer to this question is of course that the Japanese government will definitely rise up to help them. (Reuters, 3rd)

Hindenburg Airship Flies Over the South Atlantic, Headed Straight for Brazil 76

(London) The world's largest new airship, the Hindenburg, is now flying to South America on its maiden voyage. According to a Reuters special correspondent on board, it had flown over the equator at midnight. The only ship seen en route was the Hamburg-American Line mail ship Mount Amyann, which was sailing to Hamburg. The Hindenburg flew over the ship at teatime, and passengers on both ships shouted greetings to each other. At 6:18 AM this morning, the Hindenburg had flown over the island of Fernando de Noronha, belonging to Bahia, in the South Atlantic. (Reuters, 3rd)

Gravesend, England. The famous aviator Mrs. Mollison set off from here at 5:30 this morning, flying to the capital of the Union of South Africa, attempting to break the record set by British aviator Ross last month, which was three days, seventeen hours, and thirty-eight minutes. (Havas, 3rd)

It is said that the aircraft is extremely complete. It is reported that the wife has been in the aviation industry for many years and has repeatedly set new aviation records. Her first fame was in 1930 when she flew solo from London to Australia. (Reuters, 3rd)

The Significance of the Postal Administration of the Ministry of Communications Establishing Children's Savings 84

— Yu Feipeng

In the world, with mankind, there are children. Today's adults were once children, and today's children are the adults of the future, the people who will bear the responsibilities of the nation and society. Therefore, the cause of a nation's prosperity or decline can be said to be entirely built upon its children. There is an ancient saying: "Ten years to grow a tree, a hundred years to cultivate a person." Trees can be expected to have lush branches and leaves only after ten years of cultivation, while a person requires a hundred years. Cultivating a person requires a hundred years of effort. Is this not entirely dependent on generation after generation of children?

Today, in the 20th century, humans are fighting for their national survival with all their might, because the survival of the fittest has become a universal law of evolution. Without a strong nation, there is no hope for its kind. Many nations in the world have fought bloody battles for years to seek their liberation or to open up their territories, all for the sake of their descendants and to seek survival for their national seed.

When a nation is in a state of utter weakness, the only hope is to revive or restore it with trepidation. There are many ways to recover. In the past, King Goujian of Yue was almost destroyed by King Fucha of Wu. Fortunately, King Yue came up with various methods to wash away his shame. The first method was ten years of "breeding" and ten years of "teaching." "Breeding" means making efforts in terms of "quantity," and "teaching" means putting effort into "quality."

According to general surveys, there are about 100 million children in the country, which is a considerable number compared to other countries. From the perspective of "quantity," we can look upon one side of the world with heroic spirit, but from the perspective of "quality," we cannot help but retreat three houses compared to European and American countries!

When it comes to methods of cultivating children, various countries have many plans and programs. The Soviet Union has promulgated a small five-year plan for children, and various countries around the world have also designated dates as Children's Day. Everyone is celebrating and having fun. China naturally feels the need as well, and the need seems even more serious and urgent.

The work of Children's Year can be divided into three aspects: first, children's health, with the goal of enriching "quantity"; second, children's education, with the goal of enriching "quality"; and third, children's protection and relief, with the goal of taking both "quantity and quality" into consideration, with special attention to protecting children who encounter misfortune. Among the measures implemented during Children's Year, it was also stipulated that "children's thrift and savings associations" should be organized. Now we want to briefly explain this intention.

Regarding the tools of our human survival, Dr. Sun Yat-sen’s teachings once mentioned the four major elements of clothing, food, housing, and transportation. In ancient times, human life was simple, and these four elements did not seem so important. However, as times change and civilization evolves, these four items have become indispensable. What are the necessary conditions to maintain these four elements? It goes without saying that they are the three elements mentioned in economics: first, land; second, labor; and third, capital. Simply put, money is the exchange representative of capital.

For a primary or middle school student who does not have the ability to produce, the relationship with money is not very significant, because most of their lives are entrusted to their father or brother. Therefore, they do not know where the money comes from, whether it comes from hard work or bloodshed. They spend it as soon as they get it. Although we cannot say they squander it like dirt, at least they do not know how to practice thrift to seek future happiness.

Now, for the sake of the future happiness of more than 100 million children across the country, our Ministry of Communications has specially established a "Children's Savings" scheme within the Postal Savings Bureau. The fund is very solid, the interest rate is particularly favorable, and the procedures are kept as simple as possible, so that every child can enjoy this benefit. Even the smallest children can ask their school teachers to handle it on their behalf. A few cents or a few dimes can be saved at any time. For example, if you can save three copper coins a day on candy and snacks, you can save 30 cents a month, and you can save more than three yuan a year. Plus the congratulatory gifts from your parents or relatives and the interest from the post office, wouldn't you have a large sum of money after a few years of graduation?

People in society often have a slogan, which is: "Money is omnipotent." If you want to realize your hopes or achieve your career, without money, it cannot be effective. The only hope for children is to have the opportunity to study, from elementary school to middle school to university. If you are in a family that can afford to go to school, you may not feel any difficulties, but in our country, there are probably several times more children from lower-middle-class societies who drop out of school and cannot afford to go to school! (According to surveys, there are approximately 100 million children nationwide, but only 12 million are in school.) If every child can understand the principle of saving, starting from elementary school, their parents or elders can give them a necessary hint of saving, or constantly encourage their interest in saving, wouldn't it be possible to solve their admission, further education, or adult career problems?

The fact that crimes in society are generally committed for money is a very common phenomenon. However, if we carefully examine the reasons for a person's poverty, half of it is due to the inability to endure hardship, and half of it is due to the unwillingness to be thrifty. On the other hand, it is also because their desires are too high. In order to satisfy their desires, they develop all kinds of bad habits such as extravagance and dissipation. If children can cultivate the virtue of thrift and usually know the principle of saving, they can cope with money easily when they need it, and they will not feel the famine of poverty! This is a motive for the Postal Administration of the Ministry of Communications to establish children's savings.

This year is Children's Year. Our Ministry of Communications has no other way to celebrate with you. We only hope that all children and the parents, siblings, and school teachers of the children will urge you to develop saving habits from today's Children's Day onwards and realize your great plans. We cheer:

Long live the children's savings system!

Long live Children's Year!

Long live the Republic of China!

Page 11

Key Suspects in the Wang Jingwei Case, Yu Likui, Etc., Officially Questioned by Hong Kong Government; Prosecuting Lawyer States the Case; Nanjing Requests Extradition 85

Hong Kong correspondence, Yu Likui (also known as Li Zi'an, also known as Li Shiru), Zhou Shiping, Hu Dahai, and Zhang Zhihan, four persons, were previously arrested by the Hong Kong government. On November 1 of last year, Wang Jingwei, the President of the Executive Yuan of China, was assassinated. Yu and others are suspected of being accomplices. The Nanjing government learned of this and sent a letter to Hong Kong requesting their extradition for trial. The defendants pleaded not guilty and hired lawyer Xian Bingxi to represent them. The Hong Kong government hired lawyer Shi Duzhili to appear in court as the prosecutor. The case has been questioned several times. On the afternoon of March 30, at 2:30 p.m., Magistrate Shi Gaofei Lu again brought the case to court. After the court opened, lawyer Shi Duzhili said that this case had been delayed for a long time and should now be tried. There are four defendants in this case, and they should be tried together. Lawyer Xian Bingxi agreed. Then lawyer Shi Duzhili stated the case, roughly saying, "The government accuses the defendants of intending to commit the crime of assassinating important Chinese figures Jiang Jieshi and Wang Jingwei. Although this action was initiated by other political figures, as far as this case is concerned, the four defendants should bear the blame. In other words, they are bound to a certain existing organization that intends to brew riots. In 1934, the first defendant

Yu Likui met a man named Wang Yaqiao in Shanghai. This person was a key figure in the organization and had planned several incidents, some successful and some unsuccessful, and had killed several people. In 1934, they fled to Hong Kong. At the same time, other people joined the organization. The joiners did not know what they did. However, they were very friendly with Wang Yaqiao and Yu Likui. In previous interrogations, a witness testified that the defendants had traveled to many places in 1934 and 1935, but he did not know what they were doing. At the beginning of 1934, a large reward was offered for the assassination of Jiang Jieshi and Wang Jingwei. Very few people knew about this, only two or three people. The former defendant Yu Likui was one of them. As for the source of the reward, they kept it secret. Apart from two or three people, no one in the bureau could find out. Between June and July 1934, a man named Hua Kezhi came to Hong Kong from Nanjing to discuss the establishment of a news agency in Nanjing. The first defendant Yu Likui also attended. Later, the news agency was named Chenguang. The purpose of establishing this agency was nothing more than to use the privileges of journalists and photographers to get close to various important people in order to take action. By September 1934, the Chenguang News Agency was established. The president was Hua Kezhi, and the editor was He Boguang, who is now detained in Nanjing. Others include Zhang Yuhua and Liu Shurong. As for Sun Fengming, he was registered as a journalist. After the registration procedures of the agency were completed, everyone proceeded to design the murder of Jiang Jieshi and Wang Jingwei and planned to act on November 1. The Kuomintang Congress was held on that day, and all the important figures attending had to gather for a photo. At this time, all the guards had to leave their posts, and the photographers could approach the important figures because they had passes, so they could approach the important figures at will for the convenience of their work without being obstructed. Therefore, the murderer could take this opportunity to draw his gun and aim. Before the establishment of the Chenguang News Agency, they had discussed who to send to carry out the assassination. Later, Hua Kezhi proposed, and Sun Fengming was selected. During the discussion in Hong Kong, they also decided that if Sun Fengming did not have enough courage, the third defendant would be replaced.

Hu Dahai goes there, and Hu often volunteers for this. On November 1, 1934, the Kuomintang Congress was held, and Sun Fengming went as ordered. He had the opportunity to carry out the assassination, but the meeting was changed temporarily. Although Sun met Jiang Jieshi, he was a little timid because it did not match the scheduled time to act, and he returned disappointed. Hong Kong was very dissatisfied when they learned of this. They did not trust Sun Fengming very much. At the same time, they planned to send the third defendant Hu Dahai instead. After several discussions, it was decided to give Sun Fengming another opportunity. However, in order to encourage his actions, he was specially summoned to Hong Kong to listen to the instructions of the person in charge and to ask him whether he was willing to continue working. At that time, Sun Fengming came to Hong Kong with Zhang Yuhua and stated at the meeting that he was willing to continue serving. The person in charge then decided to act again on November 1, 1935. At that time, Hua Kezhi came to Hong Kong to report on the progress in Nanjing and asked for money. The second defendant

Zhou Shiping has also been to Shanghai and Nanjing to inspect the news agency and study whether Sun Fengming has made up his mind. At 8:30 a.m. on November 1, Sun Fengming went to the Kuomintang headquarters to wait until the central committee members took a photo. Sun fired three shots at Wang Jingwei, but he was eventually knocked down by the guards and injured by gunfire. Both were sent to the Central Hospital for treatment. The next day, Sun died of his injuries. Before he died, he made a confession, pointing out many accomplices. After Sun's death, the police found a photo and a reporter's pass on him, and immediately went to the Chenguang News Agency to search the premises. When they arrived at the agency, everyone in the agency had fled, and the documents were burned. A large pile of paper ashes was left, but the police still picked up a piece of scrap paper, on which were written the names of Wang Jingwei and a low-level staff member. The staff member was a registrar for the Chenguang News Agency, but this matter had nothing to do with him. After the unsuccessful assassination of Wang, Hua Kezhi came to Hong Kong to report the whole story in detail and raise money to help those who were arrested and imprisoned. At that time, several people in Hong Kong, along with Sun Fengming's wife, brought a large sum of money from Hong Kong to provide relief, and the first defendant, Yu Likui, was the main person in charge. The second defendant Zhou Shiping provided material assistance. As for the third defendant Hu Dahai, he worked very hard to run around and devoted himself the most. The police found a large number of documents at his place, proving his actions. The fourth defendant

Zhang Zhihan is Wang Yaqiao's most trusted secretary and once went to Nanjing to investigate the financial expenditures. A lot of documents were found on the third defendant, including Wang Yaqiao's handwriting. There was also a letter of repentance in the documents, saying that he was very ashamed of this failure and that he would surely be able to get what he wanted in the future. The content talked about taking pictures and had words such as "shocking the world." After the statement, Qu Di, the secretary of the Government Secretariat, testified that he had received the official document from Nanjing. The official ordered that the case be adjourned for further trial.

Record of the Public Trial of the Wang Case (4) - The Second Day of Trial of the Three Accused, Li, Xiang, and Lu - Further Investigation of Evidence Required, Trial Adjourned 86

Earlier Departure from the Chenguang Society: Asked when did you leave the Chenguang Society? Answer: October 30th. Asked why was it necessary to leave? Answer: Originally, Li Huaicheng asked me to go to Shanghai together, but because the exit permit was not obtained, I didn't go. Now that I have explained it clearly, I left. Asked what did you talk about on the evening of October 28th? Answer: That was after dinner, casual conversation after drinking. We talked a lot. Sun Fengming talked about patriotism, and Hua Kezhi expressed his support. Li Huaicheng asked me to go to Shanghai. Asked, weren't you discussing international issues and national affairs? Answer: I don't remember. Asked, they have all confessed, and Li Huaicheng just confessed too. How can you deny and say you don't remember? Answer: I don't remember now. Asked, didn't you encourage Sun Fengming? Answer: I didn't encourage him. I didn't tell him to go kill someone. Asked, so you knew he was going to assassinate someone? Answer: He didn't say for sure who he would assassinate. Asked, didn't they talk about assassinating President Wang? At this point, the presiding judge summoned the accused Li. Li said, "These were just exaggerations by young people." The presiding judge refuted him, saying, "Even if they were exaggerations, you can't deny that you didn't know." Answer: I was drunk and confused at the time. They said they wanted to warn someone, but I didn't know who they wanted to warn. Asked, according to you, you have nothing to do with this case. Why did you move two or three times after arriving in Shanghai? Answer: For convenience. Asked, where did you live after arriving in Shanghai? Tell me. Answer: I originally wanted to live at Li Huaicheng's house, but because there was no bed, I first stayed at the Andong Hotel. The next day, because I was visiting Mingyou, I moved to the Chunjiang Hotel, and later moved to a hotel on Carter Road. Asked, didn't you meet Hua Kezhi after the incident? Answer: Yes. He said that he originally wanted to kill Chairman Chiang, but he didn't know how he killed President Wang. I even said that they shouldn't have done that. Asked, according to you, you knew that Hua Kezhi instigated the assassination. He is a good friend of yours, and you lived together for two or three months. How could he not have told you beforehand? Answer: He didn't express any intention. I was always on guard against being used by them.

Received Twenty Yuan Afterwards: Asked, he gave you twenty yuan and told you to leave, is that right? Answer: Yes. Asked, what day did you leave Nanjing? Answer: The 31st. Asked, did you know about escorting Sun Fengming to the Central Party Headquarters? Answer: I didn't know. Asked, you all left Nanjing after the meeting on the 28th. As soon as you left, the incident happened, and it happened three times in total. The process was very complicated, and there was a background. You lived in the society, ate in the society, and left secretly. Today, you just deny everything and want to overturn the case. Don't say that the court can't believe you, I'm afraid you yourself can't believe it. Answer: There are many coincidences in the world. Asked, can't happen again and again and again. Answer: I don't know anything. Asked, obtaining the exit permit was the means of assassination. You obtained it for them, how can you deny knowing? Answer: I really didn't know. I introduced He Poguang to obtain it.

Refuted and Left Speechless: Asked, why did you always live in the Chenguang Society? Answer: Because my life was drifting, I had no possessions, and I lived one day at a time to save some money. The presiding judge refuted him, saying, "So anyone can live in the Chenguang Society?" The accused Xiang was speechless. Asked, have you been to Fujian? Answer: I went with Li Huaicheng because a girlfriend who was not my wife was teaching there. We wanted to seek a living with Mo Ziang. Asked, have you worked in the People's Government? Answer: No. Asked, how long did you stay in Fujian? Answer: Two or three weeks. Asked, have you been there before? Answer: I have been to Xiamen before. Asked, do you know anyone in the People's Government? Answer: I don't know anyone. Li Huaicheng, Hua Kezhi, and I all went there to seek a living. Asked, do you remember what was said at the meeting on the evening of the 28th? Answer: I was drunk and confused at the time and didn't pay attention. Asked, who is Sun Fengming's person? Answer: I don't know him. I only know that he is Wang Yaqiao's person. I don't know if he came with Hua Kezhi. Asked, do you know about the gun test? Answer: I don't know. Asked, you arrived in Shanghai on the 31st, why did you leave the Chenguang Society on the 30th? Answer: Because Li Huaicheng lived in Bafutang, I lived closer to the Mengyuan Hotel. When I left, I told them that if Li came, I would say that I lived in the Mengyuan Hotel. Asked, why did you have to go to such lengths? Clearly, you knew that something was going to happen, so you moved out. Don't try to deny everything completely. Answer: I really didn't know. At this point, the presiding judge warned the accused Xiang, saying that the content of the case was very clear. It would be understandable if you denied the minor points, but don't deny everything completely. The accused Xiang still insisted that he knew nothing. Asked, have you committed a crime before? Answer: No. Asked, didn't you commit a kidnapping case in Shanghai before and were sentenced to three years in prison? Answer: No such thing. Please have the court investigate. At this point, the presiding judge announced that the interrogation was over. The time was 3:55 PM.

The Accused Lu, a Former Lawyer, More Cunning in His Denials:

The presiding judge summoned Lu Qingqi. The accused Lu was a former lawyer, so he was more familiar with the law than the other accused. His denials were also more cunning than those of the other accused. Asked, who introduced you to the Chenguang Society? Answer: I didn't join the Chenguang Society. Asked, do you know the other defendants? Answer: Yes, I know them. Asked, do you know when the Chenguang Society was organized? Answer: I don't know. Asked, when did you go to the Chenguang Society? Answer: March of the 24th year. Asked, do you know the purpose of their running the Chenguang Society? Answer: I don't know. I only knew it was an assassination organization after reading the indictment. I didn't even know when I was arrested. Asked, do you know Sun Fengming? Answer: I don't know him. I have never seen him before. Asked, why did they leave the gun at your house? Answer: In early August of last year, Guo Zhijia came to my house and brought a leather suitcase that was more than two feet tall and one foot wide, saying that Zhang Yuhua asked him to bring it to my house.

Left Suitcase, Unaware of Gun: Asked, where did he put the suitcase? Answer: On the table. I didn't pay attention. Asked, what happened next? Answer: I took it to the room and put it under the bed. The suitcase wasn't heavy. Because it was locked, I didn't know what was inside. Asked, when did you find out that there was a gun inside? Answer: Sometime during that week, He Poguang came and opened the suitcase. I also saw the gun. At that time, I showed displeasure on my face. Asked, why did he put it here? He didn't say anything. The next day, Guo Zhifeng came and took it away. Asked, is this the gun? Answer: It seemed to be a little longer. Asked, hiding a gun is a crime even if you don't assassinate anyone. Why did you let them leave it for a week? Answer: This case is a very important event. Although I saw the gun, I didn't know that they were going to assassinate President Wang. I don't know why they wanted to put it in my house. I couldn't scold them too harshly. Asked, they have tried to assassinate three times. Each time, they used a "rental notice" to indicate whether they had acted. If they hadn't acted, they would post the "rental notice" in a certain place, and then one person would send a telegram to notify them. You sent the second telegram, didn't you? Answer: There is no such thing at all. Asked, Zhang Yuhua confessed this. Answer: There is no such thing. The presiding judge then read Zhang's confession. Lu continued to deny it cunningly.

Denied Sending Telegram Notification: Asked, you said in the investigation court that you can go to the telegraph office to check the telegram. Is it your signature? If it can be found, it will naturally be beneficial to you. But which telegraph office did you send the telegram from, what day did you send it, and who did you send it to? You have to tell the court so that we can check it. Answer: I don't know anything. How can I tell you? The presiding judge then questioned Zhang Yuhua on various points. The accused Zhang generally evaded by saying he was not clear. Asked, how much money have you used from the Chenguang Society? Answer: I haven't used any. Asked, didn't Zhang Yuhua give you fifty yuan? Answer: No such thing. Asked, you confessed yourself that they gave me fifty yuan, I didn't want it, but they insisted on giving it to me. How can you deny it? Answer: No such thing. The presiding judge then presented Lu's written record from the investigation court. The accused Lu then began to answer, saying, "Zhang Yuhua came to Zhenjiang on December 27th and asked me to tour Jinshan and Jiaoshan. Because I had dampness in my feet and couldn't walk, he gave me the money. I received it at my home in Zhenjiang." Asked, did he tell you to take this money and run away? Answer: No. Asked, maybe he wanted you to leave was out of good intentions. Answer: But that wasn't the case at the time. Asked, you confessed at the Gendarmerie Headquarters that "they had a relationship with Chen Gengshu and Li Jizhu. The funds were taken by Hua Kezhi from Wang Yaqiao and then from Chen and Li. They wanted to attack central figures. I thought it wouldn't happen, so I didn't report it." Is that right? Answer: This record is unreliable. Asked, you confessed this in the Capital District Court and the investigation court of this court. Do you remember? Answer: I only said that I usually heard them say that there was someone named Sun and someone named Shen who wanted to harm military leaders, but I didn't know the plan. I have never even seen Sun Fengming. Asked, so you only hid the gun? Answer: I didn't know anything at the time, and I have been reciting Buddhist scriptures for twenty years, abstaining from killing and saving lives.

Investigate Evidence and Adjourn for Retrial: At this point, the presiding judge said, "This case cannot be concluded today. If the defense lawyers have any opinions on reviewing the case files, they can state them." The lawyers then stated their opinions separately. The presiding judge then ordered the clerk to read the confessions of the three accused, Li, Xiang, and Lu, all of which were signed. The presiding judge then formally announced that the debate could not be concluded today because further investigation of evidence and review of case files were required. The retrial will be held on a later date. Once the date is set, summons will be sent. The defendants will remain in custody. Court adjourned. The time was 5:50 PM. (End)

Songjiang - Town Chief Accused of Fraud 87

The county has been doing well in suppressing opium, but recently, the family members of opium offenders Fu Runxiang and Xu Kaiyuan, who were sentenced for failing to appear after being summoned, Fu Wangshi and Xu Gaoshi, accused Pi Yun Town Chief Ding Shilong of extorting thirty yuan under the pretext of the case in a provincial complaint. The county has ordered an investigation. On the 2nd, the county ordered the police to summon the case for investigation. The two sides gave different versions of the story. The magistrate ordered that Town Chief Ding Shilong be detained and the plaintiffs, Fu Wangshi, etc., be ordered to return. On the 3rd, another hearing was ordered. According to Ding Shilong, Fu Runxiang was a person who failed to appear after being summoned. He was ordered to be transferred to the Public Security Bureau and then to the County Government to be sentenced to six months in prison. Later, he suddenly applied for registration for self-renewal, which was exempted from criminal punishment. Therefore, he bore a grudge and was falsely accused. Moreover, when submitting the list of informants, he was inadvertently seen by others and spread abroad. Therefore, they formed a united front and conspired to frame him. The plaintiff's statements about the source of the bribe money of thirty yuan were inconsistent. The official ordered the plaintiff to post bail for investigation, and the defendant was returned to custody.

The telephones of the County Chamber of Commerce and various trade associations in the county have been reclassified, resulting in an additional monthly fee of one yuan. Recently, Chairman Cheng of the Chamber of Commerce repeatedly negotiated with the Bureau's personnel, but the Bureau stated that the regulations had already been changed and it was difficult to reverse. Therefore, the Bureau sent a letter to the Chamber of Commerce asking it to forward to the various associations (i.e., those with telephones) to collect the outstanding balance of the previous payments. Wujiang - Shengze Town Chief Strangled 91

Fu Renlin, the manager of the Jikang Qianzhuang in Shengze Town, is currently serving as the town chief. He has been working very hard in the current general inspection of opium and drugs, which has caused resentment among the people. He was strangled to death with a rope and his body was abandoned in a rice paddy near the Sujia Highway. Wuxi - Statistics on Silkworm Seed Production in Jiangsu Province 92

Due to the resurgence of the silk industry last year, farmers are very interested in raising silkworms, so all silkworm seed farms are trying to increase production. The number of silkworm seeds used this spring is 1,681,721 sheets, including 929,941 sheets of spring-made seeds in the 24th year and 751,780 sheets of autumn-made spring seeds. All of them have been inspected by the Provincial Silkworm Experiment Station for toxins. 86,477 sheets failed. The net number of qualified seeds is 1,595,244 sheets, including 876,024 sheets of spring-made spring seeds and 719,220 sheets of autumn-made spring seeds. Currently, the number of seeds sold by various farms within Jiangsu Province is 1,129,206 sheets, with 515,311 sheets ordered by the model improvement areas in various counties, 242,643 sheets sold retail to silkworm farmers, and 371,252 sheets sold to various vendors. About 400,000 sheets were exported to Zhejiang Province. The amount needed in this county is 300,000 sheets. However, recently, more than 375,800 sheets have been ordered from various farms. The model area has decided to allocate 10,000 sheets per day to supply the demand, and will find ways to order more to avoid a seed shortage panic.

Jiangyin - Adopted Daughter Commits Suicide by Poison 93

Yuan Zu'an, an employee of the Data Shipping Company outside the North Gate and a native of Nantong, had an affair with a woman surnamed Bo from Qingjiang. He had an adopted daughter named Gendi, who is 17 years old. Bo was naturally violent and often beat the girl severely. Gendi could not bear the abuse and secretly swallowed pufferfish eggs and died.

Yangzhou - Bandits Rob Farmers and Torchure the Victim 94

In Panjiachong, west of Gongdao Bridge in the Eighth District of Jiangdu, which borders Yangshou Township, seven or eight bandits suddenly broke into the home of farmer Shi Jianzhang (69 years old) the night before. They tied up Shi's wife and daughter, and tied Shi to a pillar, using candles to burn his eyes and chest to reveal the location of the hidden silver. They stole 296 yuan in legal tender, as well as clothes, ornaments, and 1 dan and 4 dou of rice, and fled away. Su Xiaotao, the security team leader stationed nearby in Huangwang Bridge, led his team to set up sentries and discovered that village officials Zhou Kui and Gu Yongkuan were harboring bandits and harming the people. Zhou Jialu, Zhou Jiashou, etc. were immediately arrested, and the rest took the opportunity to escape. On the 2nd, the team leader had already sent the village officials who harbored the bandits, along with the captured bandits, to the headquarters for interrogation.

The civilian land requisitioned for the earthwork project outside the West Gate of Yangzhou was previously discussed by the county bureau at Jinwuzhuang, where relevant district and township chiefs and former Chamber of Commerce Chairman Wang Jingting, etc. were gathered to discuss the land price issue in order to apply to the province for it. Unexpectedly, a villager surnamed Zhao, on the morning of the 2nd, led more than 200 women and children to surround Yan Mengqin of the Provincial Committee and Shu Guohua, the Bureau Chief of the Construction Bureau, who were supervising the project, demanding the land price. They were very vocal. Shu entered the city, and the county government secretary Wang Ji's and the commissioner Wang Jingting persuaded the farmers from various villages with kind words, telling them that the land price had already been applied for from the province and would be paid as soon as it was issued. Everyone then expressed satisfaction and dispersed.

Zhenjiang - Shack Burns Down, Child Burned to Death Due to Carelessness 96

The shacks outside Beidou and Daxiaochang under Dengxian Bridge in this city are close together. They are all people who make a living by hard labor and their lives are very poor. Yesterday (the 3rd) at about 10:00 AM, the adults in the family of Ge Xiuwu, a coolie in the area, were all out working, leaving only a five-year-old girl at home. The child was careless while playing with fire, causing a fire. At that time, the wind was strong, and although the fire brigades tried their best to put out the fire, it was difficult to extinguish it for a while. Twenty-nine shacks were burned down, and Ge's child was burned to death on the spot. Although the loss was not significant, they were all poor people, and their suffering was unbearable.

Issued Written Statement Stating the Mission of the Trip, Scheduled to Return to Shanghai and Visit Beijing on the 4th of Next Month

Since the establishment of the Republic of the Philippines, it has been striving to develop various undertakings of the new country. A delegation of members of Congress has been specially sent to organize a study tour to visit China and Japan. Another news study tour, which was invited by the Japanese authorities, traveled with the delegation. It passed through Shanghai on the Japanese ship Chichibu Maru yesterday afternoon and left for Japan on the same ship last night. The details are as follows:

Three Delegates

The study tour organized by the Philippine government consists of three members of Congress. The list is as follows: Guillermo Villanueva (head of the delegation), Pedro Vera, Manuel A. Alzate, and their families. After the Chichibu Maru arrived in Shanghai, the delegates were accompanied by Mr. Wang, the manager of the China Prosperity Bank in this city, to disembark and tour. That evening, they boarded the original ship and set sail at 12:00 AM. They are scheduled to return to China on the 4th of next month for a week-long tour. The itinerary is as follows: On the 5th, they will go to Beijing. On the 7th, they will return to Shanghai. On the 8th, they will go to Hangzhou. On the 10th, they will leave Shanghai for Hong Kong. The delegation also carries many letters, which they will personally present to our government authorities when they come to China next time.

Written Statement

When the delegation arrived in Shanghai, it issued a written statement as follows: This delegation was organized by colleagues elected by the Congress by order of the government. The purpose is to study whether the markets of China, Japan, and the Far East and Europe are suitable for the sale of our country's products, so as to improve commerce and industry. The delegation also represents the people of our country to extend sincere congratulations to your country. The Chinese living on the Philippine Islands are very friendly to the people of our country. China and the Philippines began trading one hundred years ago. We hope that the relationship between the two countries will become closer in the future.

Establishment of Consulate Not Yet Determined

According to the delegation, in addition to studying commerce, they will also visit other undertakings. As for the establishment of a Philippine consulate in China, it must be approved by the Congress in Washington and has not yet been determined. As for organizing a trading company, it will be decided after we have completed our study and reported to the government.

Another news study tour came with the delegation, consisting of eight members. The list is as follows: P. Calica (head of the delegation), G. Leano (Financier), M. Concepci6n (poet), etc.

New National Atmosphere

According to Icasiono of the delegation, he told the Central News Agency reporter that the delegation was invited by the Japanese press. The itinerary is the same as that of the members of Congress. Since the establishment of the independent government of the Philippines, President Quezon has been working hard on construction, sparing no effort. Various administrative facilities are also making progress. Recently, it was also stipulated that people over the age of 20 will generally receive military training, which began on April 1. Now the Philippine government is autonomous in everything except foreign affairs. Icasiono continued, the Philippine press is still relatively developed. There are 12 daily newspapers, written in English, Spanish, and Italian. There are 40 weekly publications. There are also 4 Chinese-language newspapers founded by Chinese. The Forum News, to which I belong, has a daily circulation of 35,000 copies. This trip will be about a month later, and I will come to China again for investigation.
