Fundraising for Warplanes to Celebrate Birthday: Deadline End of June 100

Aviation Association to Move into New Headquarters on May 5th; Executive Committee Held 31st Regular Meeting Yesterday

The Chinese Aviation Association convened its 31st Executive Committee meeting yesterday (the 3rd) at 2:30 PM. Attendees included Wang Xiaolai, Wu Tiecheng, Lin Kanghou, Zhang Huichang (represented by Jin Zhaoji), Huang Bingheng (represented by Li Dachao), and observers Yao Xijiu and Hui Yijing. Wang Xiaolai chaired the meeting, with Chen Cheng recording. Secretary-General Yao Xijiu reported on the 30th Executive Committee meeting. Resolutions included raising one million yuan in Shanghai to celebrate Chairman Chiang's 50th birthday, purchasing ten warplanes as a gift, and entrusting provincial and municipal governments and branches of the association to handle the matter, all of which are being actively promoted. Telegrams have been received from various provinces, cities, and branches regarding the progress. Reports were also given on the China Aviation Society's handling of sightseeing flights, the construction of hangars and land leases, the application for approval of flight training courses and admission guidelines, the establishment of a library, and various expenditures for the new headquarters. Following this, various proposals were discussed: 1. Regarding when to move into the nearly completed new headquarters and how to prepare, it was resolved to hold the move-in ceremony at 2:00 PM on May 5th and to appoint Yao Xijiu, Li Dachao, and Jin Zhaoji to handle the preparations. 2. Regarding whether the association's organization and budget should be revised based on actual needs due to the increasing complexity of its affairs, it was resolved to prepare a proposal for discussion at the next regular meeting. 3. Regarding which banks should manage the funds collected from various locations for Chairman Chiang's birthday, it was resolved to designate the Central Bank of China, Bank of Communications, and Shanghai Municipal Bank as custodians, and to request Lin Kanghou to negotiate interest rates with each bank. 4. Regarding whether to submit a comprehensive plan for purchasing warplanes for the birthday celebration to the Aviation Committee, it was resolved to approve the proposal. 5. Regarding setting a final deadline for submitting donations for purchasing warplanes for the birthday celebration to facilitate centralized transfer, it was resolved to order the aircraft four months in advance, and that donations should be centrally collected by the Aviation Association and remitted no later than the end of June. 6. Regarding sending personnel to inspect the provincial branches and simultaneously promote the idea of national salvation through aviation, it was resolved to request President Wang or an Executive Director and Secretary-General Yao to go, with the departure date set for May. 7. Regarding how to prepare for convening a National Aviation Conference, it was resolved to set the conference dates from October 1st to 5th, and to appoint Wang Xiaolai, Wang Zhengting, Lin Kanghou, Yao Xijiu, and Li Dachao to handle the preparations. 8. Regarding the Naval Aircraft Manufacturing Bureau's request to promote the domestic production of trainer aircraft and asking the association to order ten aircraft, it was resolved to refer to the fourth proposal and request Secretary-General Yao and Director Zeng Yijing to liaise with the Aviation Committee to make a decision. The meeting adjourned at 5:00 PM.

Further news: The Fundraising Committee for Purchasing Warplanes to Celebrate the Birthday, to concentrate efforts and complete the mission of purchasing warplanes for the birthday celebration as scheduled, sent letters to all entertainment venues and movie theaters in the city, requesting that they donate all their revenue from one designated day. The committee received a reply from the Xin Ji Grand Stage yesterday, stating that this year marks Chairman Chiang's 50th birthday, and that the Chairman's hard work and great achievements are deeply supported by all the people. During this grand celebration, it is appropriate to express our congratulations. The theater will do its best to help and will notify the committee when the performance date is decided, requesting that the committee send personnel to supervise the ticket revenue. The enthusiastic support of the Grand Stage is admirable. The committee has sent a letter of thanks, urging them to make greater efforts, and hopes that other theaters and entertainment venues will follow suit to jointly accomplish this great undertaking.

Further news: The Salted Fish Trade Association's donation for purchasing warplanes to celebrate the birthday has been reported previously. Their donation of 200 national currency yuan was sent to the association yesterday for counting. Also, the local Candle Trade Association held a meeting the day before yesterday, stating that although the industry is in a severe slump, they should still make a small effort to purchase warplanes to pray for Chairman Chiang, expressing their respect. The enthusiasm of the industry in supporting the revolutionary leader and celebrating is evident.

National Products Sales Cooperative Association Resolves to Participate in International Exposition 101

Lin Kanghou Discusses the Purpose of Sponsoring the Association

People from various circles, both Chinese and foreign, are actively preparing for the Shanghai International Exposition to revive the city's declining economy. Preparations are underway separately, and the construction of the exhibition site has already begun and is expected to be completed by the end of May, with the opening on July 1st. Many Chinese and foreign manufacturers have been contacting them to participate in the exhibition, and exhibits from various places have been shipped to Shanghai one after another. The China National Products Sales Cooperative Association held a regular meeting yesterday afternoon and resolved to notify all member factories nationwide to participate. Details are as follows:

Resolution to Participate

The China National Products Sales Cooperative Association held a regular meeting at the Zhengyi Society of the Continental Department Store yesterday at noon. Over fifty directors attended, including Cai Shengbai, Hu Xiyuan, Fang Yixian, Wang Zhixin, Fang Jiange, Wu Qingtai, Pan Yangyao, Sun Ruihuang, and Wang Zhengfang. The meeting was chaired by Wang Zhixin. In addition to discussing association affairs, the chairman proposed the issue of the association's members participating in the Shanghai International Exposition. After discussion, it was resolved that the association, organized by legitimate Chinese and foreign merchants, with a pure purpose, should notify all member factories to participate in order to promote national products.

Letters to Members

In accordance with the resolution, the association sent letters to all member factories yesterday, stating: "We are writing to inform you that Mr. Dulu, a foreigner residing in Shanghai, and Mr. Tang Shuping, a Chinese merchant, plan to hold the Shanghai International Exposition from July to the end of August this year on Yangshupu Road in the western suburbs of Shanghai. The scale is grand and unprecedented. We have heard that many products from Britain and the United States have been added, and it is expected that the number of visitors will be considerable. Recently, representatives from the expo contacted the association and warmly welcomed Chinese manufacturers to join the exhibition. At the last regular meeting, it was resolved to send a letter to all member factories to solicit participation. The association stipulates that each unit occupies 196 square feet (14 feet long and 14 feet wide), with an exhibition hall 9 feet high. The rental fee for each unit for two months is 430 national currency yuan, and 530 yuan for corner locations (including water, electricity, and room fees). If more than four units are rented, the association can provide design and construction services free of charge. If members can rent several units together, they may be able to request a discount on the rental fee. If your factory agrees to participate, please inform the association of the number of units you intend to rent as soon as possible so that we can gather the information and contact the expo on your behalf. This is to notify all member factories. China National Products Sales Cooperative Association."

Lin's Remarks

Mr. Lin Kanghou, Secretary-General of the Shanghai Bankers' Association, stated that the Shanghai International Exposition held in Shanghai is sufficient to save the city's economic decline. In addition to expressing his sympathy, he also listed his name in support. According to Mr. Lin, the earliest supporter of the association was Guo Bingwen, Director of the International Trade Bureau. He conducted a detailed investigation of the purpose and economic status of the expo's organizers. According to Mr. Guo, the earliest organizer, Dulu, came to Shanghai to select a vacant lot at the old site of the Sanxin Yarn Factory on Yangshupu Road as the expo site. His purpose was to promote products and expand trade. Mr. Guo believes that its purpose is pure, and that such an exhibition is indeed beneficial during this period of industrial and commercial depression. After investigating its economic status, it is also very reliable. For national product factories with group guarantees, rent is not collected in advance, and the method is also very appropriate. In addition to personally listing his name in support, Mr. Guo also sent a letter inviting him to list his name in support. After receiving Mr. Guo's invitation, he also conducted an investigation and learned that the organizers of the association are Tang Shuping and Dulu. Mr. Tang is a wealthy merchant in Shanghai, and the purpose he proposed is supported by the industrial and commercial sectors. The association only collects the rental fee from participants at the opening, and national product factories are protected. The method is quite appropriate, so he also agreed to support it. He believes that any exhibition, if the economic source does not rely on rent, the planning is proper, and the management is appropriate, will be of great benefit to the sale of national products.

The 23rd Year 6% British Boxer Indemnity Bonds: Principal Repayment Lottery Held Yesterday 102

A Total of 265 Bonds Drawn for Principal Repayment of £57,000; Payments to Be Made by the Central, China, Communications, and HSBC Banks Starting July 1st

The fourth principal repayment lottery for the 6% British Boxer Indemnity Bonds of the 23rd year of the Republic of China was held at 10:00 AM yesterday in the conference hall on the third floor of the Central Bank. Xu Kan chaired the meeting. Attending as monitoring representatives were Lin Jinyu from the Auditing Department, Wu Qiding from the Ministry of Finance, Zhang Jingzhi from the Ministry of Railways, Lu Shuping from the Shanghai Municipal Government, Lin Kanghou from the Bankers' Association, Shen Jingliang from the Money Trade Association, Ma Jiliang from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, as well as Xu Kan, Chairman of the Bond Fund Committee, and committee members Jiang Lufu, Zhou Kai, Ma Xier, and Gai Shili, and lottery staff Huang Dazhong from the Central Bank, Zhu Qizhen from the Bank of China, Luo Qiyuan from the Bank of Communications, and Ai Xu from HSBC, totaling over twenty people.

Chairman's Report: The meeting began as scheduled. He expressed his sincere thanks. This time, 74 bonds of £50 should be drawn in the British bond lottery, divided into the first and second groups, with each group drawn from ten cylinders. 153 bonds of £100 should be drawn, divided into the third to sixth groups, with each group drawn from ten cylinders. 38 bonds of £1,000 should be drawn, forming the seventh group, also drawn from ten cylinders. Winning Numbers: The lottery was then executed. The meeting adjourned at noon.

Bank Clearing House Expands Operations and Increases Total Amount 103

Acceptance Bills, etc., Have Begun to Circulate in the Market

The Bank Clearing House, affiliated with the Shanghai Bankers' Association Joint Reserve Committee, was established on January 10th of the 22nd year of the Republic of China. After a successful trial operation, it gradually expanded. In addition to the member banks of the Bankers' Association, the China-One Trust Company and the Four Banks Savings Society are also members of the clearing house. Since reaching an agreement with the Money Trade Joint Reserve to collect money shop bills and after the Central Bank joined, the clearing volume has increased. For example, yesterday's total amount was 31,340,339.09 yuan, the clearing amount was 10,211,190.02 yuan, the transfer amount was 18,821,305.07 yuan, the amount for money shops was 1,738,488.14 yuan, and the amount for others was 1,177,611.49 yuan. The Bank Acceptance Bill Exchange was established on March 16th of this year. The member banks, totaling 38 including China and Communications, have all signed a convention. The member banks have submitted the collateral stipulated in the regulations to the evaluation committee of the exchange for review. In accordance with the convention, the exchange will sign and accept the bills. These bank acceptance bills have already circulated in the market. All sectors are happy to accept them due to their well-known credit. At the same time, the exchange handles discounting. Yesterday, the discount rate for 90-day bank acceptance bills was 1.2 cents per thousand yuan per day. Re-discounting is handled by the Central, China, and Communications banks. It is heard that the exchange will gradually expand its operations after a successful trial run, with the aim of rescuing the market and increasing credit chips.

Qiu Yujin Discusses the Dutch Currency Devaluation: A Good Opportunity to Promote National Products in Nanyang 104

Hopes to Establish Promotional Organizations as Soon as Possible; Also Hopes the Government Will Open Shipping and Banking Services

Qiu Yujin, a Chinese merchant from Nanbang Port, Su Island, Dutch East Indies, has returned to China to investigate the actual situation of domestic products in order to develop the sales of national products in Nanyang. Mr. Qiu entered Beijing via Guangdong and Fujian last week, met with Chen Shuren, Chairman of the Central Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission, and Wu Dingchang, Minister of Industry, and made all the necessary arrangements. He arrived in Shanghai on the 2nd and is staying at the Cangzhou Hotel. He will visit the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and the China Industrial Foreign Trade Association to make arrangements, and plans to return to Nanyang next week.

Excellent Opportunity to Promote National Products

A reporter from the New Voice Society interviewed Mr. Qiu at his residence. According to him, the Chinese in various ports of the Dutch East Indies have gradually understood the situation in their motherland since last year through publicity by the government and overseas Chinese merchants such as Hu Wenhu, and the import of domestic products has also gradually increased. Chinese who used to run Japanese goods have switched to running national products, so the sales of national products are gradually developing. There is a great demand for domestic canned foods, cement umbrellas, flour, ironware, and other items. Since the devaluation of the Dutch currency, with each Dutch guilder worth two national currency yuan, it is an even better opportunity to import national products. Therefore, it is hoped that domestic industries will make efforts to promote sales in Nanyang as soon as possible in order to obtain overseas markets.

Japanese Goods Are Now Seeking Rapid Development

In the past, Japanese goods were promoted in Nanyang by relying on the sales of Chinese commercial shops and did not establish their own shops. Only wholesale firms were operated. Since the Chinese switched to operating national products, the Japanese, seeing the danger of market seizure, have successively established their own shops. The scale is not large, and it is still difficult to compete with Chinese shops. The overseas Chinese initially agreed not to purchase Japanese goods, but Japanese goods rely on domestic shipping and the economic adjustments of the banking sector, so the transportation is rapid and the cost is extremely low, which is unmatched by our overseas Chinese.

Urgently Hoping to Realize Three Types of Undertakings

Therefore, the overseas Chinese in Nanyang now hope that the motherland's government and the banking and commercial sectors will realize three types of undertakings as soon as possible: opening shipping routes to Nanyang to directly transport national products to Nanyang and get rid of the constraints of foreign shipping; establishing large-scale banks to adjust overseas Chinese finance; and establishing national product promotion organizations so that overseas Chinese merchants do not have to travel long distances to return to China to purchase goods.

Living Conditions of Overseas Chinese in Su Island

Su Island is under the jurisdiction of Dutch Java. It is an important and commercially prosperous location. The annual output of native products such as pepper, coffee, and coconut dried goods is very large. There are more than 310,000 overseas Chinese on the island, 40% of whom are engaged in commerce, and the rest are working. Life is relatively stable, but in society, due to the national strength, although there are so many overseas Chinese, they are not as powerful as the small number of overseas Chinese from other countries. Therefore, when incidents occur, the local government is inevitably somewhat biased. The Dutch government still charges each overseas Chinese an entry tax of 150 guilders, equivalent to 300 national currency yuan, and a uniform import tax of 30%.

Resolution of Rickshaw Dispute: Vehicle Operators Resume Business This Morning; Shanghai Municipal Council Vehicle Committee Reaches Agreement with Vehicle Owners Yesterday; April Licenses Available for Collection from 6th Onward; Mutual Aid Society Fees Payable by the End of This Month 107

Mr. Zhong Si, the General Manager of the Shanghai Municipal Council, Mr. Massey, Chairman of the Vehicle Committee, and Mr. Yin Zhiling, representative of the vehicle operators, held discussions at the Shanghai Municipal Council Vehicle Committee at 11:00 AM yesterday. As a result of the discussions, the vehicle operators agreed to resume rickshaw services from this morning, operating as usual. April licenses can be collected from the 6th of this month. The mutual aid society fees can be paid by the end of this month, without the need to prepay them at the same time as license collection. The above conditions were all signed and agreed to by Yin Zhiling, Gu Songmao, and Hou Shao'an, representatives of the Vehicle Operators Association, to be followed accordingly.

Temporary Meeting

After Representative Yin reported back to the association, the vehicle owners considered the negotiations satisfactory. Subsequently, an emergency meeting was held at 4:00 PM, resolving that: Negotiations were successful, and business will resume on the morning of the 4th; All unlawful rickshaw pullers who dragged away vehicles and handed them over to the police will have their vehicles retrieved by the respective vehicle owners upon presentation of their licenses; The police are requested to investigate missing vehicles; Rickshaws on the streets that are incomplete or damaged should be detained by the police at any time, and the owners notified to retrieve them to avoid losses; Statistics on the number of losses should be compiled; and April licenses should be collected and business resumed immediately.

Losses on Both Sides

According to the person in charge of the Rickshaw Pullers Association, speaking to the Xin Sheng News Agency reporter yesterday, the business suspension of three days resulted in a loss of 21,600 yuan in vehicle rental fees. Losses due to damaged vehicles and missing items amounted to over 26,000 yuan, totaling approximately 50,000 yuan. According to Chen Guoliang, the representative of the rickshaw pullers, the loss for the rickshaw pullers during the three days, with two pullers per vehicle per day, at one yuan per person, totaled 60,000 yuan.

Southern District Announcement

The French Concession Police Department summoned more than ten representatives from rickshaw businesses and rickshaw pullers in the French Concession's special district at 9:00 AM yesterday, holding a joint meeting in the police station. As a result of the discussions, to avoid escalation, it was decided to first allow the vehicle operators to resume business and release vehicles as usual. As for the issue of opposing rent reduction, vehicle operators can negotiate with the Shanghai Municipal Council again after resuming business. After the meeting adjourned at 10:30 AM, the French police immediately posted an announcement regarding the resumption of business by vehicle operators at the entrance of the Southern District branch of the Rickshaw Pullers Mutual Aid Society, stating: "Announcement: The public rickshaw operators in the French Concession have decided to resume business today. All rickshaw pullers can directly rent vehicles from the original vehicle owners or contractors as usual, to make a living. Please be informed accordingly."

Notice of Resumption of Business

The Special District Office of the Shanghai Rickshaw Operators Association announced yesterday: "Upon investigation, the Rickshaw Committee decided to implement new regulations from April 1st, forcibly collecting mutual aid fees and restricting the registration of rickshaw pullers. The rickshaw pullers, based on their own interests, declared a cessation of mutual aid fee payments. The vehicle operators believe that the rent reduction issue is relatively minor, while the issues of restricting rickshaw puller registration and forcibly collecting mutual aid fees not only greatly affect the livelihoods of the rickshaw pullers but are also deficient in legal principles. It is difficult for us to act. Therefore, we were forced to temporarily suspend business from April 1st, awaiting a resolution. However, this suspension of business was purely a peaceful negotiation, especially with the concern for maintaining the rickshaw pullers' livelihoods in mind. After the suspension of business, we repeatedly tried our best to maintain the issue of relieving the rickshaw pullers' living conditions. Unexpectedly, a portion of rickshaw pullers, under the leadership of the Mutual Aid Society, engaged in excessive actions and disruptive events, which was truly unexpected and deeply regrettable. Now, the Shanghai Municipal Council authorities deeply feel that prolonging this suspension will impact social security and the rickshaw pullers' livelihoods, which are all concerning. They negotiated with the representatives of this association to find a solution, deciding to postpone the payment of this month's mutual aid fees, collect 2.09 yuan to receive April licenses, and continue to process the registration of rickshaw pullers. This association believes that this result has achieved the initial intention of the vehicle operators in suspending business to protect their livelihoods. For the sake of social prospects and the rickshaw pullers' livelihoods, we should first resume business. As for other issues, we will negotiate separately. In addition to separately advising all vehicle operators to unanimously resume business from today, this association deeply apologizes for all disruptions to social traffic and inconveniences to passengers during the suspension of business. As for the April licenses, this association has already paid for them. All vehicle owners who have paid the donation to the Shanghai Bank should bring their payment receipts from April 5th onwards, first to this association for verification and license collection. Fearing that this may not be fully known, this announcement is specially made."

Vehicle Operators' Statement

The person in charge of the Vehicle Operators Association made a statement to the Xin Xin News Agency reporter yesterday, stating: "The vehicle operators' suspension of business originated from opposing the Shanghai Municipal Council Vehicle Committee's implementation of new regulations from April 1st. The main points of these new regulations are threefold: Forcibly collecting mutual aid fees; Restricting the registration of rickshaw pullers, which is detrimental to the livelihoods of tens of thousands of unemployed rickshaw pullers; and Reducing rental fees without reducing the mutual aid fees. We believe that the rent reduction point is secondary. The vehicle owners and rickshaw pullers have a relationship as close as lips and teeth, which is extremely important. If accumulating business can sustain vehicle operators, we are happy to support rent reduction. However, the two [registration restriction and mandatory fees] are related to greatly limiting rickshaw puller registration, immediately causing tens of thousands of rickshaw pullers to be unemployed due to not being registered. The Mutual Aid Society has been established for twenty months, collecting 300,000 yuan from the rickshaw pullers' hard-earned money, but with little achievement. The rickshaw pullers, seeing this obligation without rights and no possibility of continued burden, declared to this association their refusal to pay and requested that all vehicle operators not prepay. This association believes that the payment of mutual aid fees by the vehicle operators is essentially a collection on behalf of payment and must be based on the principle of mutual agreement. Now that the payers have expressed their refusal, the vehicle operators cannot make the payment on their behalf. However, the Shanghai Municipal Council is ordering compulsory collection, placing the vehicle operators in a difficult position and wanting to avoid the risk of having their licenses revoked or fined a large sum by the council. They were forced to temporarily suspend business from April 1st, awaiting negotiations. After the mutual suspension of business, the vehicle operators repeatedly tried to maintain the rickshaw pullers' livelihoods. Unexpectedly, a portion of rickshaw pullers, under the leadership of the Mutual Aid Society, engaged in excessive actions and disruptive behavior, which is deeply regrettable. On the morning of the 3rd, at 11:00 AM, Mr. Zhong Si, the General Manager of the Shanghai Municipal Council, felt that prolonged delays would have a major impact on social prospects and the livelihoods of the poor. He negotiated with Mr. Yin Zhiling, the representative of this association, to find a solution. After consulting with Mr. Massey, Chairman of the Vehicle Committee, it was decided that: Payment of the April mutual aid fees would be postponed, and licenses would be issued for 2.09 yuan, allowing for business operations; and the registration of rickshaw pullers would continue. This association believes that solving the two major problems of mutual aid fees and rickshaw puller registration fulfills the association's initial intention of protecting the rickshaw pullers' livelihoods, so we can express our agreement. We have already notified all vehicle operators to resume business immediately. However, during the suspension period, we are deeply grateful for the warm sympathy and assistance from party and government agencies, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the Chinese Ratepayers Association, all Chinese directors, and people from all walks of life. This association deeply apologizes for all disruptions to social traffic and inconveniences to passengers during the suspension period."

Cancellation of Relief

The Rickshaw Pullers Mutual Aid Society issued a notice to its members: "Notice: According to the resolution of the board of directors of this association yesterday, since most members of this association currently have no rickshaws to pull, this association intends to provide each member with one jiao and five fen of silver dollars per day from April 4th to maintain their livelihood. This proposal has been approved by the custody committee, and all procedures have been prepared, awaiting implementation. However, we have now received news that the vehicle operators will resume renting vehicles as usual from April 4th. Therefore, we are specially notifying all members to resume rickshaw pulling work as usual. The above relief is no longer necessary, and this association is deeply fortunate that the members' livelihoods can return to normal and not be cut off, which is more perfect than the above relief provided by this association."

Mutual Aid Society Letter

The Shanghai Rickshaw Pullers Mutual Aid Society issued a correction letter, stating: "Sir, recently your newspaper has carried news related to our association, but some of the reports are untrue, and the truth is unclear. We hereby request that the following corrections be made: Our association is an organization for the welfare of public rickshaw pullers in the International Settlement. Its internal organization and work have long been known to all walks of life. Social undertakings are already difficult to manage, let alone the difficult situation and numerous obstacles faced by our association. However, we do not slack off in our work because of this. If it is said that all our work is only for the enjoyment of one or two hundred people, then any rickshaw puller can prove the enthusiastic participation in our five clinics, six bathhouses, six children's schools, mutual aid department, and other projects. People from all walks of life can also come and inspect in person to understand the truth. In addition, our work has statistics, and all receipts and expenditures have accounts, procedures are solemn, and the organization is strict. How can our association fabricate facts to cover the eyes and ears of the people of the world with one hand? As for the current organizational charter, it was decided by the Shanghai Municipal Council, and how can our association intervene? A few people, without investigation, say that our association once instigated rickshaw pullers to forcibly drag vehicles, or that many rickshaw pullers came to the association to cause trouble. All of these are unfounded. Since the April 1st suspension of vehicle release, our association has sincerely comforted and persuaded the rickshaw pullers to seek a proper solution with peaceful means. At the same time, the board of directors of our association also convened a special emergency meeting and resolved yesterday (2nd) that from the 4th, all members of the association who have no rickshaws to pull will be given one jiao and five fen of silver dollars per day to temporarily maintain their livelihood. The locations are as follows: Upstairs of the Xiaocaichang Market on Dongjiaxing Road; Gordon Road Police Station; Public Works Department of the Shanghai Municipal Council on Yuezhou Road. Every other day, from 8:00 AM to 5:00 PM, they will receive it once, that is, three jiao of silver dollars each time. It will be stopped when most vehicles have been released. In short, our association will do its best to assist as much as possible, and our association is also deeply concerned about social order and tranquility. This is addressed to the gentlemen of the Shen Bao Newspaper."

Explanation from the Zhejiang Provincial Government on the Difficulties of Issuing New Bonds, Telegram Sent to the Shanghai Banking Association Yesterday 108

The Zhejiang Provincial Department of Finance issued new public bonds to reorganize old debts, with a total issuance of 60 million yuan. The bond regulations and the principal and interest repayment schedule have been drafted by the Department of Finance and passed by the Zhejiang Provincial Government's meeting. Director of the Department of Finance, Cheng Yuanfan, took them to the capital to submit them to Finance Minister Kong for review. The specific plan for reorganizing old debts has also been changed and finalized. The central point of the change is to divide the old seven public bonds issued by Zhejiang Province into four types (A, B, C, and D) for collection and reorganization. The repayment period is also divided into four periods: 14 years, 16 years, 18 years, and 20 years. Type A is the Highway Public Bonds and the Repayment of Old Debts Public Bonds, with a repayment period of 14 years and an annual interest rate of one percent, now reduced to 0.9 percent. Type B is the Construction Public Bonds and the Disaster Relief Public Bonds, with a repayment period of 16 years and an annual interest rate of 0.8 percent, now reduced to 0.7 percent. Type C is the Clearing Old Debts Public Bonds and Treasury Bills, with a repayment period of 18 years. The annual interest rate of the Clearing Old Debts Public Bonds is 0.8 percent, now reduced to 0.7 percent, while the monthly interest rate of the Treasury Bills remains unchanged at 0.5 percent. Type D is the Local Public Bonds, with a repayment period of 20 years and an annual interest rate of 0.6 percent, which remains unchanged. After reorganization, each public bond will still be calculated at 100 yuan. Whether the lottery will be drawn evenly each year has not yet been determined. However, in order to maintain credit, the 13th Construction Public Bond and the 9th Treasury Bill lottery for principal and interest payments at the end of April will still be handled according to the original plan. As for the portion of the loan collateralized by the Shanghai-Hangzhou banking industry, the Department of Finance will negotiate individually and handle it separately. The following is the telegram sent by the Zhejiang Provincial Government to the Shanghai Banking Association: (Omitted Title) Since the 16th year of the Republic of China, Zhejiang Province has undertaken construction projects, with huge expenditures. After the elimination of taxes, income has decreased significantly. In recent years, it has also suffered from disasters, and tax revenue has been even shorter. Budgetary income and expenditure have not been balanced, and the annual deficit has always relied on borrowing to make up for it. To date, the total amount of bonds issued, unpaid principal, interest on various loans, and funds to be allocated amount to more than 57 million yuan. The depth of accumulation is undeniable. It is estimated that the debt burden to be paid in the 25th year amounts to more than 11.11 million yuan. The amount is so large that it exceeds one-half of the total annual income of the province. Currently, when preparing the budget, debt expenses cannot be shortened, and various administrative expenses cannot be reduced. Since income is difficult to meet expenses, the budget cannot be established, and even the originally designated debt fund is unavoidable. If we do not take timely measures to reorganize, it will be difficult to continue to maintain. Rather than losing credit in the future, we should plan in advance. The provincial government is planning to reorganize debts this time, not only to alleviate financial difficulties, but also to stabilize future credit. It has already transferred the Department of Finance to consider and handle the issuance of reorganization public bonds. The issue of postponing interest reduction will be considered in detail, taking both sides into account. The loan portion will also never unilaterally abolish the original agreement. At this time of local financial crisis, the people and the government are closely related. Your association manages the city's finances and hopes to discuss it in detail to maintain the overall situation. Please inform and forward to all bondholders for their information.

Abstract of the Shanghai Municipal Council Budget for the Year, Ordinary Current Revenue Over 24 Million, Total Revenue Over 22.41 Million Yuan 109

The 1936 budget table of the Shanghai Municipal Council has now been prepared, printed, and bound into a book, ready to be submitted for approval at the annual meeting of foreign taxpayers on the 15th of next month. The content is roughly divided into two major parts: ordinary and education. Since there is no proposal to levy additional education expenses this year, all funds for education will be allocated under the education budget item as usual.

Under the Ordinary Section's Current Revenue Item, there are: Land Tax 6.92 million yuan, House Tax 10 million yuan (a decrease of approximately 988,800 yuan due to the economic recession), Special District House Tax 770,000 yuan (also a decrease of more than 80,000 yuan), Special Advertisement Tax 35,000 yuan, Wharf Tax 500,000 yuan, License Tax 3.13 million yuan, Rental Income from Shanghai Municipal Council Properties 397,000 yuan, Public and Municipal Industry Revenue 2,133,360 yuan, Miscellaneous 746,640 yuan. The total of the above nine items is 24,451,200 yuan. After deducting the education expenses of 2,367,500 yuan from the above total and adding the surplus carried over from last year of 269,740 yuan, the net revenue is 22,414,240 yuan. After allocating 2 million yuan to the reserve fund, the total is 24,414,240 yuan.

Under the Ordinary Section's Current Expenditure Item, there are: Military [Various Teams and Russian Volunteer Corps] 690,140 yuan, Fire Department 1,149,870 yuan, Police Department 9,901,640 yuan, Health Department and Hospitals 1,622,720 yuan, Donations and Subsidies to Charitable Organizations 483,900 yuan, Public Works Department 5,372,490 yuan, Shanghai Municipal Council Band 126,500 yuan (from January to May this year), Public Library 15,750 yuan, Finance Department 1,129,620 yuan, President and General Manager's Office 492,190 yuan, Legal Department 141,410 yuan, Chinese Affairs Department 100,800 yuan, Intelligence Department 66,800 yuan, Factory Group 57,960 yuan, Rickshaw Affairs Committee 53,400 yuan, Ordinary Expenses 1,561,300 yuan, Interest and Commissions 1,200,370 yuan, Repayment of Bond Certificates 156,610 yuan. The total expenses of the above departments is 24,331,670 yuan, plus 65,690 yuan for the purchase of goods and equipment in various departments, totaling 24,397,360 yuan. The surplus of current revenue and expenditure is 16,880 yuan.

Ordinary Section Temporary Revenue and Expenditure Items, Under the Ordinary Section's Temporary Revenue Item, there are: Surplus from other sales 1.3 million yuan, Miscellaneous Revenue 50,000 yuan, Funds raised through public bonds or other temporary measures 12 million yuan. After deducting the temporary education expenses of 64,740 yuan to be allocated, the net income is 13,328,5260 yuan.

Under the Temporary Expenditure Item, there are: Shortfall from last year 5,592,000 yuan, Ditches and Canals 285,500 yuan, Wharf 7,000 yuan, Land Purchase 171,500 yuan, Houses 719,500 yuan, Roads 1.95 million yuan, Machinery and Equipment 86,000 yuan, Endowment Fund Tailings 700,000 yuan, Fund for Repaying Public Bonds 3,753,500 yuan. The total of the above items is 13,326,500 yuan. The surplus of temporary revenue and expenditure is 20,260 yuan.

Budget Table of Education Expenses for This Year. Under the Education Expenses Section, the Current Revenue Item includes: Surplus carried over from last year 41,130 yuan, Funds allocated from the Ordinary Budget's Current Revenue Item 2,367,500 yuan, and Miscellaneous 10,000 yuan. The total of the above is 2,418,630 yuan, which is an increase of more than 76,000 yuan compared to last year. The funds allocated from the Ordinary Current Revenue Item also increased by approximately 97,000 yuan compared to last year. This year's education expenses account for approximately 1.86% of the total donations and the equivalent amount of property tax.

In terms of Current Expenditure, there are: Education Committee, Education Department, and Purchase of Supplies, totaling 71,380 yuan, Expenses for Western Schools 600,9170 yuan, plus 3,630 yuan for the purchase of equipment, 14,000 yuan for housing, 84,340 yuan for ordinary expenses, 177,460 yuan for interest, 180,000 yuan for subsidies to Western schools (the total expenses for Western schools, including subsidies to Japanese schools, is 1,068,600 yuan), Expenses for Chinese Schools under the Chinese Directors 652,090 yuan, plus 9,910 yuan for the purchase of equipment, 21,940 yuan for housing, 115,550 yuan for ordinary expenses, 251,400 yuan for interest, 227,760 yuan for subsidies to Chinese schools (the total expenses for Chinese education, including subsidies to private schools, is 1,278,650 yuan). The total current expenditure of the above education expenses is 2,418,630 yuan.

Under the Temporary Revenue Item, the funds allocated from the Ordinary Temporary Revenue Item amount to 64,740 yuan. This amount is sufficient to pay for the construction of various schools and the addition of machinery and equipment.

The second phase of issuing opium smoking licenses in this city began on the 1st. All smokers in this city should apply for registration and license renewal at the sub-bureaus and patrol teams in their place of residence. The deadline for license renewal is May 31st. Those who fail to renew their licenses after the deadline will be prosecuted by the Songhu Garrison Headquarters for smoking without a license. The Municipal Public Security Bureau believes that the license renewal has already begun. It is feared that many smokers in this city still do not thoroughly understand the significance of license renewal and the penalties. In order to prevent the foolish people from testing the law, it has been specifically decided that from today, it will cooperate with the Municipal Anti-Smoking Committee to organize a propaganda team to adopt a citywide district propaganda system. Teams will be dispatched within the jurisdiction of each sub-bureau to distribute propaganda materials to the public and give open-air lectures to awaken the public's attention. Last year, the Municipal Public Security Bureau organized the registration of smokers. The citywide register of smokers has been completed by the bureau and submitted to the Municipal Government for forwarding to the Military Commission for review. There are a total of 30,833 smokers in the city, with a citywide population of 2,028,814 people. On average, there are 15 smokers per thousand citizens. From this statistic, it can be seen that there are many smokers in this city. Ministry of Finance Instructions; Preferential Coupons Do Not Need to Be Stamped 117

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce previously telegraphed the Ministry of Finance to inquire whether preferential coupons should be stamped. Yesterday, they received a reply from the Ministry of Finance, Tax Department, No. 9074, which stated: "The telegram and attachments have been received. After investigation, the preferential coupons issued by Yong Tai Chang are used as a standard for profit distribution based on the number of transactions recorded on the coupon, and customers still pay in cash when purchasing goods. This is different from the account books used to withdraw goods, as stated in Item 5 of the tax rate table. Therefore, they do not need to be stamped. However, these preferential coupons are only allowed to record the amount of each transaction and must not include the name and quantity of the goods in order to prevent any trickery. You are hereby instructed to comply accordingly." This instruction.

A Report on the Exhibition of New Handicrafts on the German Round-the-World Giant Ship – Sports Equipment and Various New Literary and Art Supplies, as well as Models of Trains, Cannons, and Silver Airplanes – The Revival of Germany is Certainly Not Accidental 122

(Special Report from this Newspaper) The annual world tour ship has become a very fashionable trend in recent years. Major European and American shipping companies are trying to figure out the psychology of passengers and are making meticulous designs, using excellent giant ships and special arrangements to ensure that passengers do not feel bored or lonely during long voyages. This time, the German Hamburg America Line's world liner, the Reliance, is such a plan.

Touring Shanghai

The Reliance, from New York, USA, via the Atlantic and Mediterranean to the Far East, arrived in Shanghai yesterday. The voyage has lasted 86 days, and two-thirds of the 40,000-mile journey has been completed. The 232 members toured Shanghai yesterday, and this morning they must set sail for Qinhuangdao to visit North China, explore the scenic spots of the Great Wall, and admire the greatness of the ancient palace. Then, they will follow Japan, cross the Pacific Ocean, and return to the United States, which will require another 53 days of voyage before returning to New York.

Handicraft Exhibition

It is heard that Hamburg America Line and North German Lloyd are the two major shipping companies in Germany. This time, the world ship is dispatched to the Reliance, which is the first time to the Far East. The equipment and decoration of the ship are beautiful and magnificent, and it can really surpass the "Queen Mary". After arriving in Shanghai, in order to facilitate the members to get on and off, it specially docked at the Gonghexiang Wharf in Hongkou. Because there is an exhibition of new German handicraft products in the ship, the reporter obtained a visiting certificate in advance and went to the ship for sightseeing at 11:00 AM yesterday.

Spring Breeze Like Scissors

Not many visiting certificates were issued for this exhibition, and the time was limited to 10:00 AM to 12:00 PM. In the spring breeze like scissors, the reporter went to Gonghexiang Wharf by car with unlimited hope. He saw a white giant ship like a palace on the sea, already docked. The coolies on the pier were busy loading and unloading goods from the Ewo and Tonghe ships, and the sound was endless. At the docking place of the giant ship, there were piles of bronze porcelain jade wares leather goods, colorful and all over the ground. These are all antique dealers taking the opportunity to catch customers, hoping that the tour members will buy their items.

Start Visiting

When the reporter boarded the ship, he was greeted cordially by the crew at the entrance. Most of the visitors to the ship were Westerners, and there were only a few Chinese. The Chinese and Westerners who came to the ship mostly came with the same purpose: to visit the exhibits. A crew member led me through the magnificent hall and dining room, over two decks, to the highest Su Deck, and then began to visit the exhibits.

Sports Equipment

What is displayed on the upper deck is completely sports equipment, with hundreds of items. The reporter is a layman to sports. Football basketball racket ball tennis are all available. Each category has the name of the factory and instructions, but all are in German. A crew member performed and explained the racing boat, the push-pull machine used to practice arm strength, and the freehand exercise equipment. Then he went to the exhibition room of handicraft products, which contained all the items used in the latest garden houses. The crew member also pointed out that this material has been used in the "Reliance" ship to install the "New Era" room, which is strong, beautiful, and both.

Literary and Art Supplies

Secondly, he went to the literary and art supplies exhibition room. Almost all stationery and supplies are available, and all are novel. The most important are Montblanc fountain pens and pencils. There are a total of two hundred and several kinds of fountain pens, and there are also more than seventy kinds of pencils. There are also new-style leather notebooks, exquisite and elegant, which have not been seen at sea. As for the newly produced porcelain and glassware in Germany, they are arranged on the table, one category per table. One type is similar to cloisonné, but without flowers. There is also an agricultural product exhibition room, all of which are pure steel hoes, or three-bend hooks, or five-pointed rakes, which have never been seen in China, all Wol brand.

Trains and Cannons

Finally, visit the new-style train model, another room is arranged, and the room is equipped with upper and lower intersecting circular railway lines, and car routes. The train is divided into electric vehicles and steam vehicles, a total of four or five kinds, and the cars are also divided into several categories, all Ma klin brand. The manager turned on the motor, the pole lights in the railway were all lit, and each train flowed around, up and down staggered, and galloped. The cars also rushed up and down, but the car road was all three tracks. In the railway room, there were also displayed large cannon models, which can automatically go up and down, armored tank models, and cavalry models, which are military representations.

Silver Airplane

After the reporter visited this room, he was led by the crew to the front cabin to visit various different aircraft models displayed, including seaplanes, passenger planes, and other application planes, each with a number, and the body was silver. All are hung in the middle. In addition, there are Siemens' new products of machine parts and supplies. At this time, the reporter was dazzled and unable to see everything. Because the time had reached twelve o'clock, he resigned and returned on the way. Nian Germany's revival is really not accidental.

Zhou Shimin Sued by Maid for Obscenity Case; After Mediation, it is Known to be Settled; Yesterday's Continued Hearing Approved Withdrawal 123

Guangdong merchant Zhou Shimin is a major shareholder of the Shanghai China Insurance Company. His family lives at No. 10 Fen'anfang, Dongxi Huade Road, Public Concession. Last month, Zhou was suddenly sued in the First Special District Court by a Ningbo woman named Zhang Jinxiu, who worked as a maid in his house, for the crime of obscenity. The general idea of her complaint is: Zhang Jinxiu has been working as a maid in Zhou's house. She is over the age of maidenhood and has a pretty appearance. Zhou Shimin saw her beauty and inevitably had ulterior motives. He took the opportunity to seduce her, but because his wife's surveillance was very strict, it was difficult to fulfill his wishes. Last spring, Zhou's wife gave birth, and the defendant was like a turtle escaping its shell, chasing the plaintiff. At that time, the defendant was still addicted to bad habits and was lying down all day alone with the lamp. He took the opportunity to seduce her under the pretext of asking the plaintiff to load cigarettes. He used sweet words, coercion, and inducement to the best of his ability. At that time, the plaintiff was also temporarily weak-willed and fell into his trap, and was raped. Moreover, she became pregnant because of this. Unexpectedly, good things are more tortuous, and the spring is leaked, and Zhou's wife found out. The voices of opposition rose. Zhou saw that things had reached this point and there was no way to deal with it, so he ordered Zhang Jinxiu to leave temporarily to avoid his edge. How could he have never heard from the defendant since then. Now Zhang Jinxiu is nine months pregnant, and for the sake of the piece of meat in her belly, she had no choice but to file a lawsuit, and asked the court to quickly summon the defendant Zhou Shimin to court for punishment according to the law, et cetera. The case has been approved by the court, and has been summoned and heard once. Because the defendant did not appear, the continued hearing was rescheduled to the 26th of last month. At that time, Zhou Shimin still did not surrender, and only entrusted lawyer Wei to appear in court, representing the statement that the defendant had just returned to Shanghai from Suzhou and suddenly suffered a cold, so he could not appear in court. He presented two prescriptions to the court on the spot and requested a reschedule. However, the plaintiff's lawyer then stated that the defendant had indeed personally gone to the law firm to handle the settlement procedures, but because the two sides were too far apart, they had not been able to reach an agreement. Now that he suddenly claimed to be sick, it was close to a pretext to evade. He should ask the court to issue a warrant for arrest. Then the judge Jiang Shuzi turned to question Zhang's purpose of filing the lawsuit. Zhang Jinxiu immediately proposed in court, requesting the court to order the defendant Zhou Shimin to pay a total of 11,190 yuan for living expenses and children's education expenses. At that time, the court warned her that it was not yet known whether Zhou Shimin was guilty, and it was not appropriate to demand such a large amount of money. However, because the defendant did not appear, there was no way to hear the case, so he declared that it would be rescheduled once again, and the continued hearing would be held on April 3, and Zhou's lawyer was ordered to inform the defendant that he must appear in court at the next hearing, otherwise he would be arrested. At 3:00 PM yesterday, the date of the continued hearing arrived again. Judge Jiang still sat in the first criminal court for the hearing. In addition to Zhang Jinxiu and the original defendant's lawyer, Zhou Shimin still did not appear in court. At that time, the court prohibited the public from listening to the hearing because the case involved obscenity, so the details of the hearing are not clear. However, it is reported that the mediation has been agreed in the second reschedule, so the court approved the withdrawal of the request from both parties at the same time yesterday, and the court ruled that Zhou Shimin was not guilty. A storm can be announced to be quelled.

The Amicable Insurance Company Held a Shareholders' Meeting Yesterday 131

The Amicable Life Insurance Company held a shareholders' meeting at 4:00 PM on the 3rd of this month (Friday) at its head office at Number 17, The Bund, Shanghai. The shares represented by the shareholders present exceeded the legal quorum. The meeting was chaired by General Manager Meng Fu, whose report briefly stated that although the general economic situation in China last year was not very good, the company's business still showed progress. The amount of insurance, the amount of reserves, and the assets all increased. The current total amount of insurance has reached 59,846,000 yuan, a record for the company. The liability reserve reached 6,601,274.14 yuan, an increase of more than 1,000,000 yuan compared to the previous year. As for the total assets, they were 7,204,795.67 yuan at the end of 1934, but increased to 8,305,866.50 yuan at the end of December last year. The total amount of new insurance added last year reached 12,462,189 yuan, of which 5,437,881 yuan were established in China, and 7,024,308 yuan were established in Annam, Malaya, and the Philippines. Therefore, in terms of new policyholders added last year, China saw a slight decrease, while other regions increased by 10%. (Omission) Furthermore, due to the failure of certain things in Shanghai last year, the company's investment suffered some losses. However, these losses were all covered by the company's reserves, so they will not affect the policyholders' reserves, nor will they damage the company's capital. Therefore, policyholder dividends can be paid as usual without any changes. This report can be said to be the end of the company's nineteenth year of operation. From the perspective of policyholders, this kind of achievement is very satisfactory. First, there is no change in the policyholders' dividends. Second, the company's economic strength is very strong. Even from the perspective of shareholders, it is very gratifying, because after the company is properly managed and the internal affairs are solid, even if the public reserve suffers a slight loss, the company's credit and the goodwill of the policyholders will definitely increase.

Wang Shubao, Owner of the Xiang Stage, is Accused of Murder; the Cause is a Love Triangle Involving Actress Yu Yanfang; Five Years After the Incident, the Deceased's Mother Discovered the Truth and Sued in Court 132

In a house at No. 100 Zhangjia Lane Road, Zhabei, during the chaos of the January 28th Shanghai Incident in the 20th year of the Republic of China, a person named Ji Zhongtang from Hai'an, who was a detective in the former Municipal Police Bureau, was shot and killed by a group of rioters. Ji was injured and died on the spot. After the war subsided, the Police Bureau discovered two suspects in the case and sent them to the local court for interrogation. However, due to lack of corroborating evidence, they were released. Five years later, the deceased's family repeatedly investigated and learned that the main culprit in Ji's murder was a certain Wang, the owner of the Xiang Stage Theater. They filed a lawsuit with the local court prosecutor's office, requesting an investigation and punishment according to the law, in order to redress the injustice for the deceased. The court accepted the lawsuit and issued a summons for Wang, but he could not be found. Therefore, an arrest warrant was issued. A detailed report of the case is as follows:

The Shooting

The victim in the case, Ji Zhongtang from Hai'an, was in his thirties and had been a detective in the former Municipal Police Bureau. He was dismissed from his position due to a case and sentenced to two years and six months in prison by the local court. He was released from prison at the time of the January 28th Shanghai Incident in the 20th year of the Republic of China. A friend of Ji's, a certain Sheng, and Yu Yanfang, an actress from the Xiang Stage Theater (from Zhenjiang, specializing in female roles, in her twenties), once had a love affair and lived together with great affection. Later, Yu Yanfang became a concubine. Yu Yanfang was eager to break away from her relationship with Sheng, but Sheng insisted on not wanting to, and a dispute arose. Sheng complained and threatened to harm Yu Yanfang. Before long, Yu Yanfang was walking alone one night and was attacked by a group of hooligans who threw excrement at her. A person named Zhou was arrested on the spot and sentenced to two years and six months in prison by the court. Zhou appealed to the Suzhou Higher Court, but before the case could be concluded, Zhou died of illness in prison. The matter between Sheng and Yu Yanfang remained unresolved and was about to become a stalemate. Ji, posing as a peacemaker, planned to mediate. He went to the Xiang Stage Theater to meet with Wang Shubao and Yu Yanfang to discuss the matter. However, on the way, he was lured by a group of rioters into the kitchen of a tea house owned by an old woman named Wei Chen in No. 100 Zhangjia Lane Road, where they threatened him with guns and shot at him. The bullet hit a vital spot, and Ji died on the spot. The perpetrators fled without a trace after the incident. At the time, only Zhang Xiaowanzi, who lived nearby, witnessed Ji's tragic death.

Innocent Suspects

After the war subsided, the deceased's family reported the case to the Police Bureau. Two suspects, Zheng Xiaoheizi and Shi Zitou, were arrested and sent to the local court for interrogation and then transferred to the criminal court. It was repeatedly heard that the court summoned them, but since Ji's family had no sufficient evidence to present, Zheng and Wang were found not guilty due to insufficient evidence and were released. Ji's mother was heartbroken that her son had been brutally murdered and the injustice had not been redressed. She repeatedly investigated and learned that the mastermind behind the murder was Wang Shubao, the owner of the Xiang Stage Theater (from Hai'an, in his fifties) on Middle Dalu Road. The cause was a love triangle involving Yu Yanfang. She invited Zhang Xiaowanzi, who had witnessed the incident, to testify and filed a lawsuit with the local court prosecutor's office, requesting an investigation and prosecution according to the law.

Arrest of the Mastermind

The court approved the lawsuit, and the prosecutor ordered an investigation. Ji's mother requested in court that an arrest warrant be issued for Wang to be brought to court for questioning. The prosecutor approved the request. The arrest warrant was dispatched to the French police station. The police were waiting for the warrant and, at around 6:00 PM, turned to the police station for assistance. They rushed to the Xiang Stage Theater on Middle Dalu Road to arrest him. The suspect Wang, fearing punishment, fled upon hearing the news and could not be apprehended. The police reported the situation to the court, and the court has issued an arrest warrant and is determined to investigate the matter.

According to reliable sources, the Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administration, in order to facilitate spring travel for tourists, has decided to operate special express trains for spring tours between Shanghai, Hangzhou, and Zhaokou every Saturday and Sunday from April 4th to May 3rd, and also on April 10th and April 13th (one round trip each). Children's Year Children's Day 152

— Kong Xiangxi

The designation of April 4th as Children's Day was initiated by the China Child Welfare Association. Now we are approaching the fifth observance. It coincides with the nationwide expansion of the Children's Year movement. Provinces and cities across the country are holding grand celebrations to awaken the public to the importance of promoting children's welfare, revitalizing the nation, and ensuring the prosperity of the country. This is the foundation.

Today's children are the masters of the nation's future. Confucius said: "The young are to be regarded with respect." A Western philosopher said: "The progress of national civilization follows in the footsteps of children." All of this can illustrate that children are the life of the nation, the source of civilization, the vitality of the country, and the essence of society, and cannot be ignored. Therefore, in this context, we have boundless hope for today's Children's Day. The celebration of Children's Day has even greater significance.

Only by nurturing healthy individuals can we have a healthy society. Only with a healthy society can we have a healthy nation. Therefore, in recent years, I have promoted this idea within our association and made it clear to the people of our country. Unfortunately, the work of child welfare is still in progress, but foreign aggression continues unabated. The foundation has not been strengthened, but it has been destroyed first. The strength has not been increased, but it has been hit again. Looking ahead, I am deeply apprehensive! To seek national salvation, we should start from the root and first cultivate the children on whom the life of the nation depends. With ten years of replenishment and ten years of education, we can educate and nurture the majority of children in the country. National difficulties can be resolved, foreign aggression can be permanently eliminated, and our 5,000-year-old Chinese nation can always stand tall and independent in the world.

The prosperity and decline of a country are determined by the quality of its children's education and upbringing. Therefore, the significance of Children's Day in this Children's Year is undoubtedly extraordinary and self-evident. Taking advantage of this period, let us further clarify its meaning as follows: It must be understood that children are the children of the nation, not the private property of their parents. Therefore, the nation should be responsible for their education and upbringing. Looking at European and American countries, they have established various institutions for child care to fulfill their responsibility of educating and raising children. This is one meaning; Children's education and upbringing must have equal opportunities, regardless of their wealth or poverty, and whether they have parents or not. They should all be able to get what they need, without worrying about food and clothing, and they should all be able to learn and develop their talents. We should start well and end well, so that they can become healthy individuals, to secure society and strengthen the nation. This is another meaning. I hope that all capable people in the country will promote this idea, encourage society, and urge the government to develop the cause of child welfare and build a long-term plan for cultivating talents! If we can do this from now on, national difficulties can be resolved, and foreign enemies will never be seen again. The Children's Day that we Chinese people celebrate today will not be in vain!

Educating Children and the Future of the Nation 153

— Wu Tiecheng

Children are the seeds that perpetuate the life of the Chinese nation. The survival, prosperity, and decline of the Chinese nation's future depend entirely on today's children; whether today's children have a promising future depends on today's parents, today's society, and today's government. Therefore, today's parents, today's society, and today's government should earnestly take on the responsibility of caring for and educating children. Caring for and educating children is not just a matter for one family or clan; it has a great impact on the future of the nation and the country. As the saying goes, "Care for your own young, and extend that care to the young of others." So, we care for children, not just our own children. The National Government designated this year as Children's Year to make the people of the whole country aware of the importance of children to the nation and the country. At present, the general public in our country seems to have a too shallow concept of the nation, while their concept of the family seems to be too deep. If we can transfer the concept of planning for the family to planning for the nation, I dare to believe that the Republic of China and the Chinese nation would not have suffered such an unfortunate encounter today. Even if we have such an unprecedented crisis today, we can have the strength to overcome this danger and break through this difficulty. Unfortunately, the people of the whole country are still only planning for their own family, clan, and surname, and cannot plan for the entire nation and country. Therefore, although China has 450 million people, accounting for a quarter of the world's population, almost as many as all the countries in Europe, it is still inevitably oppressed, bullied, and dominated by a small number of ethnic groups!

What is the reason for this? To break it down; firstly, our 450 million people are like a pile of loose sand, without unity. Everyone is planning only for themselves, for their own family, clan, and surname, and not for the nation and country. This is the first reason. Secondly, we mostly do not thoroughly understand the principle of "There are three unfilial acts, and having no offspring is the greatest." We only know about simply passing on the seed, but we do not know how to cultivate this seed. It must be known that it is useless to have many people who are not educated, and they have no power. In the world, there are often many uneducated people who are oppressed, bullied, and dominated by a small number of educated ethnic groups. Therefore, it is useless to only seek an increase in quantity without seeking an improvement in quality. Han Feizi once said: "A million ignorant people are as good as no people." Let us go to the straw huts to see our poor compatriots, and look at our coolie compatriots on the streets. They are not educated, they have no knowledge, and they have no national consciousness. The survival, prosperity, and decline of the nation and the country seem to have nothing to do with them. Let us go to the slums to see the situation of our poor children. Almost all ten children in our slums have diseases, either eye diseases or other diseases. They usually live in sewage, garbage piles, and coal cinder piles. They are not physically healthy, and they have no knowledge. How can such children have the ability and be able to raise their heads and show their faces for the nation and the country when they grow up! Ordinary people only know the superficial meaning of "There are three unfilial acts, and having no offspring is the greatest," but they do not know that if we have offspring but do not educate them well, and let them be unrestrained and unworthy, or even squander their family fortune, it is even more unfilial. Mussolini said: "The fate of the nation depends on the increase in population." Only fathers can be said to be human! This sentence, although it does not fail to be a kind of outpouring of patriotic enthusiasm, if we are in China, where the population is already very large, if we only increase the quantity without improving the quality, then it cannot be regarded as truly loyal to the country. Therefore, our greatest task today is not only to pass on the seed, but also to cultivate excellent seeds. Everyone must think about the future of the nation and the country, care for children, and educate children, so that today's children will not become the seeds of national subjugation.

The German philosopher Fichte, who revived Germany, had the same opinion as me. At that time, Germany was oppressed by Napoleon and had no way out; therefore, he loudly called on the people of the whole country to "take it upon themselves to cultivate excellent national seeds." Later, in less than twenty years, Germany was saved from the root! We must not miss today's opportunity to hope that all fathers in the country will pay special attention to this. From now on, everyone must earnestly take on the responsibility of caring for children and educating children in order to revitalize our Chinese nation! During this Children's Year, we must not only strive to promote and implement children's undertakings, but also awaken the attention of the people of the whole country, so that they will have a new concept of children; we must also awaken the children of the whole country to recognize the importance of their own position. Today they are children, and in the future they will be the masters of the Chinese nation, and they will also be the elements that continue the life of the Chinese nation.

The Shanghai Municipal Government will definitely work hard to promote children's undertakings within its capabilities, and will never dare to abandon its responsibilities; especially for the undertakings of poor children, we should pay special attention. The public housing for the poor planned and implemented last year is one example. Each poor people's village has two to three hundred or three to four hundred houses; in each poor people's village, what we pay the most attention to is the welfare of children. Our plan is to set up a simple clinic, a small school, and a children's playground in each poor people's village, so that poor children can go to the doctor when they are sick, go to school to study, and have a small garden to play in, so that they can no longer live in sewage and coal cinder piles. In addition, there is also a small children's care center. In addition, there is a poor children's nursery in Nanshi, and there are health clinics in various districts; we pay close attention to children's health and inspections, such as physical examinations for primary school students. However, children's undertakings are a great and important cause, which the government cannot do alone. The entire society and the government must work together to promote it in order to succeed. Therefore, today we must also call on the citizens of Shanghai to support the promotion of children's undertakings. (The End)

Zheng Zhaojia is still in the United States and will go directly to Europe to attend. The details of the match in Hong Kong are recorded separately below.

Xu and Lin Unexpectedly Lost in Doubles

At 11:30 AM, Xu Chengji, Lin Baohua, and others went to the Cricket Club's stadium and first played a doubles exhibition match with Cai Huiquan and Xu Weipei. The Xu and Lin team took a 3-1 lead, but the Cai and Xu team caught up and tied. The Xu and Lin team won another game and were caught up by Cai and Xu, and then won two consecutive games, defeating Xu and Lin 6-4. Due to time constraints, only one set of doubles was played. It was found that Xu and Lin's defeat was not because their ball skills were inferior to Cai and Xu, but because they were careless, resulting in an unexpected loss.

Xu Chengji Defeated Xu Weipei

After the doubles match, Xu Chengji played a singles match against Xu Weipei. A total of two sets were played. Xu won with 6-0 and 6-1. Xu's performance in this match was quite good. His serve made it almost impossible for Xu to cope. He won very easily, without losing the demeanor of a famous player.

Lin Zhen Defeated Cai Huiquan

The next match was Lin Zhen against Cai Huiquan. Cai's ball skills were not bad, but his serving skills were very ordinary, and his strength was not as good as Lin Zhen's. Therefore, after winning the first game in the first set, Lin Zhen took back five games in a row. He quickly caught up to 3-5, and Lin Zhen won the last game, so he lost 6-3 first. In the second set, Lin Zhen took a 2-0 lead. Although Cai won back two games later, he still lost 6-2 again.

The National Sports Association Announced the Measures for the Sports Observation Group to Germany 162

The quota has been reduced to ten people; registration is open from now until May 16 at the Sports Association.

Must be healthy, of good character, and proficient in one of the three languages: English, French, and German.

Pay 750 yuan for travel expenses to Germany; the rest will be subsidized by the National Sports Association.

The original quota for the sports observation group to the 11th World Games in our country was 20 people, but it was later reduced to 10 people due to financial difficulties. In addition to self-provided funds, the China National Sports Association will also provide appropriate subsidies for the expenses to Germany. The measures are as follows: 1. Quota: 10 people (male); 2. Duration: Accompany the delegation to the 11th World Games in Germany and return home; 3. Qualifications: A. Graduated from domestic or foreign universities or sports colleges; B. Have more than three years of service experience and are still dedicated to sports; C. Healthy and of good character; D. Aged from 25 to 35; E. Proficient in one of the three languages: English, French, and German; F. Should be formally introduced by their current employing institution; 4. Registration: Those who wish to participate can register at the China National Sports Association on Yanping Road, Shanghai, from now until May 16, and fill out a formal form; 5. Notes: A. A certificate of physical examination from a registered doctor should be submitted at the time of registration; B. After being admitted, half a dozen recent half-length photos should be attached immediately; C. After the observation is completed, they must continue to work hard for the domestic sports cause; 6. Subsidies: Each admitted member must pay a part of the travel expenses during the period in Germany, approximately 750 yuan in national currency. This amount must be paid before June 1. All necessary travel, food, and accommodation expenses will be borne by the Association, totaling approximately 1,500 yuan in national currency; 7. Admission: The Board of Directors of the Association will hold a meeting to review and decide.

This City's Various Circles Enthusiastically Celebrate Children's Day Today 163

Celebration Ceremony Held at the City Sports Field at 9:00 AM. Mayor Wu Gives a Speech and Receives Children's Representatives. Wonderful Performances and Abundant Gifts. Various Sectors Also Offer Special Discounts.

Today is the 6th Children's Day, coinciding with the implementation of the Children's Year. Various circles in this city have specifically arranged to hold an expanded celebration ceremony at the city center sports field starting at 9:00 AM today. Mayor Wu will serve as the chairman and present souvenirs. There will be wonderful performances. It is estimated that over 10,000 children will participate. At that time, there will be a lively and grand occasion. The details are as follows:

Venue Arrangement: The celebration ceremony will be held at the city sports field. The association has already arranged the venue overnight. All participating children will enter and exit through the main entrance of the West Rostrum. The altar is set up at the West Rostrum, decorated with red and green colorful silk and several pots of fresh flowers in front of the platform. A banner reading "Shanghai Various Circles Celebration of the 6th Children's Day Assembly" is hung high outside the main entrance. School children, labor children, and orphaned children are assigned designated areas to gather. The bus parking lot is located on Jibei Road and the square outside the West Gate. The group bus parking lot is located around the outside of the venue.

Celebration Ceremony: The celebration assembly will begin at 9:00 AM with: 1. Playing music, 2. All standing at attention, 3. Raising the flag, 4. Singing the Party Song, 5. Paying the highest respect to the national flag, the Party flag, and the portrait of the Premier, 6. The chairman respectfully reads the Premier's will, 7. Silence, 8. Chairman's report, 9. Speeches by heads of Party and government organs, 10. Speeches, 11. Reply by children's representatives, 12. Children's representatives have an audience with the Mayor, 13. Performances, 14. Dismissal. Children participating in the ceremony do not need admission tickets. Adults must be accompanied by children to enter the venue.

Assembly Staff: Presidium: Wu Tiecheng, Wu Xingya, Pan Gongzhan, Li Ting'an, Cai Jinjun, Xu Peihuang, Yang Xiaotian, Xing Wan, Jiang Jianbai, Lin Yannan, Hu Shuyi, Chen Tiesheng; Master of Ceremonies: Nie Haifan; Recorder: Chen Dongbai; General Affairs: Zhang Binghui, Jiang Jianbai, Lin Yannan, Chen Tiesheng, Xu Gongmei, Yan Wenkai, Guo Junshi; Entertainment: Hu Shuyi, Qian Fugong; Publicity: Zhu Xuefan, Zhu Chun; Security: Yin Guanzhi, Wu Menggong; Hygiene: Zhou Guobao, Wu Zhongyao; Transportation: She Miao, Huang Yueqi; Solicitation: Wang Gang, Sun Yongyi; Reception: Zhang Yueru, Chen Zhengfan; General Commander of Reception: Yuan Zengyu; School Children Reception: Wang Keyong, Sun Yucai, Wu Renya, Ding Shoutang, Xu Manxin, Wu Shiqian, Hu Zongfan, Xu Heng, Xu Qingji, Xia Changqi, etc.; Labor Children Reception: Wang Gang, Tan Shenyan, Zhu Zhenbang, Xie Chenghun, Wang Rangyu, Huang Shuji; Orphaned Children Reception: Zhang Yueru, Ding Bingnan, Zhao Jian, Zhang Wanqing; Free Participation Children Reception: Pan Xingzhong, Fu Gunian, Lei Kenan, Lin Guifu, Yang Disheng, Mei Dazai, Tai Tongxuan, Pan Hongheng; Gifts: Zhang Yueru, Yuan Zengyu, Pan Xingzhong, Xie Chenghun, Zhou Wanghe, Qian Honglie; Security Commander: Chief of the City Center Branch; Band: Public Security Bureau; Boy Scouts: He'an Elementary School; First Aid: Health Bureau.
