Motherhood Education Competition: Shanghai Women's Education Hall, in order to promote the sense of responsibility of mothers in each family and create a social atmosphere that values virtuous mothers, has specifically organized a Motherhood Education Competition on this Children's Day. After the competition, they plan to organize a Mother's Association to study the way of being a mother. All residents of this city with mothers of children aged five to ten can participate. The competition items are divided into: 1. Physique, 2. Cleanliness, 3. Etiquette, 4. Response. The order of the competition is determined by drawing lots. Those who arrive late will be disqualified from the competition. The scoring method is based on a total score of 100%. Physique is graded out of 30 points, cleanliness is graded out of 20 points, and etiquette and response are each graded out of 25 points. Those with a total score of 90 points or above will be awarded a mother's souvenir and a children's toy, reading material, and candy as encouragement.

Buck's Elderly Mother, Japan's Kikuikehiro's Father, Arishima Takeo's With the Young, etc. are all works of great contribution to parents across the country. National School Health Technology Conference Opens 169

Nanjing, 2nd. The National School Health Technology Conference, convened by the Health Department, opened on the morning of the 2nd. More than fifty people attended, including Wang Shijie, Liu Ruiheng, Dana, and Yuan Dunli. Chairman Liu Ruiheng gave a speech, stating that health education in Europe and the United States has developed rapidly, but China is relatively late. It began to be promoted after the establishment of the Health Department of the National Government, and it is now gradually taking shape. However, it is still not widespread across the country. The purpose of this conference is to seek popularization methods. I hope everyone will help each other and propose effective solutions and resolutions for implementation. Wang Shijie then gave a training speech, stating that since China began to run new education, there has never been school health work. At present, cities are developing rapidly. In the future, if the education and health agencies cooperate closely, they can give basic training to a large number of children, which will be of great help to the nation's health in the future. Finally, Professor Dana gave a speech, encouraging the development of health education in China. The meeting was adjourned at noon. In the afternoon, group discussions were held on five groups of proposals: 1. Administrative organization, 2. Rural school health, 3. Urban school health, 4. Technology, 5. University health. The meeting was adjourned at 5:00 PM.

Nanjing, 3rd. The School Health Technology Conference held a joint meeting of various groups on the morning of the 3rd. The administrative, urban, rural, university, and technology groups reported the results of their reviews, and the meeting was adjourned at 11:00 AM. In the afternoon, a discussion meeting was held. Professor Dana gave a speech, elaborating in detail on issues such as student class time, examinations, children's rest, course order, homework, student management and punishment, textbook compilation, and teachers' attitudes towards students. He also asked representatives to explain the situation in China. The meeting was adjourned at 5:00 PM.

Finance 175

Rumors Benefit Many Parties; Standard Gold Briefly Excited; Outcome Still Returns to Stability

The gold market yesterday saw silver prices rise, and raw gold prices fall, but market sentiment remained positive. This was largely due to a rumor circulating since last Saturday that a certain bank was planning to export cash. The rumor boosted buying, also because raw gold could be used as legal tender collateral. In the early morning, overseas silver markets saw London rise and New York remain stable. A very small number of Indian buyers at the 大條脚地關 (a specific location, likely a trading hub) were posting bids at the closing price. Sellers were offering at the posted price plus 0.0625, with buyers reportedly willing to wait at 0.0625 below the posted price. Forward silver prices in Montreux rose slightly. Exchange rates had begun to contract. London raw gold fell to one penny. The Central Bank's posted exchange rates revealed both London and New York were stable, and the customs gold unit remained unchanged. The standard gold price was posted at 1143.2 yuan. Off-market pre-market trading opened at 46 yuan strong, lacking sellers. Market sentiment remained positive, with major players such as 大德成, 元昌, 永福餘 all buying, driving the price up to 6.8 yuan. 福興, 永大, 大德成 then began selling, causing the price to fall to 6.3 yuan. The morning opened flat. Buying interest continued strongly after opening, leading to further increases, but many took the opportunity to sell at the higher prices. The price soon gradually declined. HSBC's posted exchange rates revealed both London and New York were stable. Prices fluctuated briefly, but a large number of large players cutting losses led to a period of weakness. After the silver equalization tax was announced to increase by half a percent, prices stabilized. Rumors continued to benefit the market, and buyers continued to be active, eventually pushing prices up again. The market was slightly erratic around noon, with a slightly flat outlook for the afternoon, although there was some brief stability. However, the final situation seemed unlikely to improve. Swap rates were posted by the long positions yesterday at five yuan. The day's market conditions are recorded below.

The morning opened at 1146.4 yuan, the same as the previous close. Although 鼎康 was selling at 6.3 yuan, 大德成, 恒餘, 春源, 永惠祥, 鼎康, 天成祥 all entered the market, with Shanghai picking up May shillings at 4375 and half a penny, pushing the price up to 6.9 yuan. 恒昌, 永福興, 永生源, 永洽豐, 永大發 all actively sold, pushing the price back down to 6.2 yuan. 愼大, 永惠祥 took advantage of the lower prices to buy. HSBC's posted exchange rates revealed both London and New York were stable, still rising to 6.7 yuan. 愼大, 永恒餘 sold, falling to 6.1 yuan. 鼎豐, 乾元, 永洽豐, 永恒餘 continued to buy at the lower prices. The silver equalization tax was announced to increase by half a percent, gradually pulling prices up. 大德成, 元豐, 永惠祥, 潤昌裕, and others also came to buy, with 惠祥 buying particularly aggressively, pushing the price up to 7.2 yuan. 同裕, 潤大豐, 恒昌, 永恒餘, and others sold, causing the price to fall to 6.6 yuan. 鼎康, 大德成 then re-entered the market at 7.2 yuan. 須茂 and others supplied at the higher prices. The noon closing price was 1147 yuan.

The afternoon market opened at 1146.8 yuan. 大德成, 景福, 鴻康, 永愼大, 永 sold, retreating to 6.6 yuan. 元茂, 永愼大, 永恒昌, 永福餘 picked up McCallum's June US dollars at 8125, rising to 7 yuan. 洽豐, 永大豐, 益成 sold, and 愼大永 cut losses, gradually falling to 6.4 yuan. 大發永 took advantage of the lower prices to buy. The closing price was 1146.5 yuan, flat after the close.

The settlement price, based on the Central Bank's standard gold price posting, fell to 1143.2 yuan, raised by 3.3 yuan according to the closing price, which was 0.8 yuan more than the previous close. The account price for this month was 1142 yuan, and for May it was 1147 yuan. The morning make-up was 1142 yuan, and the afternoon was the same price. Red gold prices were photographed at +4 yuan, for 1146.4 yuan. The spot market trend was stable, with some supply from 客帮 (a specific trading group). It is estimated that the Tianjin goods were +9 yuan, sold by 盈豐恒 to 同豐恒 at 140 taels. 烚赤 (refined gold) was also +9 yuan. 盈豐恒 had previously entered 350 taels, and 大豐恒 also entered 210 taels. In addition, 銀樓 (silver shops)帮 (groups) sold a small amount of 烚赤 to 大豐恒, at +8.8 to 9 yuan. From April to May, 盈豐恒 posted 35 yuan for 35 strips, and 生源永 posted 21 strips to 元茂永 at the same price. Afterwards, 盈豐恒, 益餘成 were willing to post, but there were no parties posting in.

Trading within the exchange was normal. In summary, 春源永, 大豐恒, 鴻康永, 康元, 昌永福餘, 天成祥, 祥豐, 洽豐永, 益成, 惠祥, 恒餘, 慶發永, and others were on the buying side. 大德成, 同泰昌, 同豐恒, 福興永, 裕新祥, 乾昌祥, 大發永, 乾元永, 生源永, 景福久大, and others were on the selling side. 愼大永, 福泰永, 恒昌永 first sold and then bought. 鴻康永, 大德成 first bought and then sold.

The day's market conditions were stable, opening in the morning at 1146.4 yuan and closing at 1146.5 yuan. The highest price was 1147.2 yuan and the lowest price was 1146.1 yuan, with a fluctuation of 1.1 yuan. As a result, the market rose slightly by 0.1 yuan compared to the previous close. The number of April strips net of public orders was 98, with 7 long positions and 1 short position. The total number of May chips was 14,588, with 61 long positions and 32 short positions. The total number of transactions was 3941 in the morning and 1176 in the afternoon.

The public order shorts who settled yesterday included 生源永 56 strips, 盈豐恒 35 strips, 永豐 7 strips. The public order longs due today included 大恒 35 strips, 惠祥, 元茂永 14 strips each, 洽豐永, 德利福興永, 大德成, 益成 7 strips each, for a total of 98 strips, settled at 1142 yuan.

Foreign Exchange Situation Only Hovering 176

The exchange market was flat yesterday, then turned dull, with prices hovering between the focus of entry and exit. In the early morning, overseas telegraphs reported that London spot was up 0.0625 recently, and forward was unchanged. 脚地 said that a very small number of Indian buyers were buying at the posted price after closing, with buyers offering at the posted price plus 0.0625, and buyers reportedly willing to wait at 0.0625 below the posted price. New York silver markets were unchanged. Montreux forward silver prices were unchanged and up 5 basis points. London raw gold contracted by one penny. The pound sterling contracted against the US dollar by 125. The pound sterling rose against the French franc by 6 pounds. The US dollar contracted against the pound sterling by 75. The US dollar contracted against the French franc by 75. The Central Bank's posted exchange rates revealed both London and New York were stable, and the customs gold unit remained unchanged. The exchange market opened in the morning with recent selling prices of British currency up one shilling two and a half pence, and five six two five against the US dollar at 30 yuan, compared to the previous close. British currency was down 0.03125, and the US dollar was flat, because the exchange rate had contracted. After opening, the 日行 (likely a specific bank) picked up July's Eastern Exchange at 102.875 to 103, with 大勞 (likely a specific financial term) hovering. Later, 上海 and others picked up. HSBC's posted exchange rates revealed both London and New York were stable. The situation gradually tightened. The silver equalization tax was announced to increase by half a percent. After that, 農工 (Agricultural and Industrial Bank) and others slightly filled. Therefore, the process was peaceful. The same was true at noon. Trading in the afternoon was relatively sparse. Banks were dealing with each other and still flat. Although Chinese merchants were slightly filling forward US dollars, banks still maintained them, resulting in an extremely mediocre process. Market prices consistently hovered between the focus of entry and exit. The closing price for recent selling prices was one shilling two and a half pence strong, and the US dollar at 30 yuan, compared to the previous close. British currency was slightly down, and the US dollar was flat. Forward was also the same, because the exchange rate declined. Banks were picking up and filling differently. 上海 had more appetite, while 農工 filled US dollars. The day's events are recorded below.

Securities 178

Large Players Aggressively Pushing Up Public Bonds, Rises Still Seem Weak

Yesterday at the Chinese Merchants Securities Exchange, market conditions continued to struggle with a weak rebound. Even with prices being pushed up, the rise still seemed weak. Observing the four types (乙, 丙, 丁, 戊) of bond being released over the past few days, only four types were being bought, apparently as a smokescreen. This has been going on for several days, and the quantity of sales greatly outnumbers the buys. Therefore, the forward prices of four of the bond types have risen a large amount in the past two days (1.20 yuan), while type 戊 has risen only 0.40 yuan. This shows that the unloading of the bonds has been organized. The sellers at the trading table acted with deliberation, whereas the buyers seemed to have an artificial air about them. The morale of the people can be seen, and there are few optimists. If the 甲 type slips even slightly, it will fall rapidly. Considering the number of disturbances and the emptiness of the peoples' hearts, it is difficult to be optimistic about the future. Otherwise, it would result in a repeat of the boring, meandering market. Opening yesterday saw types 4 and 35 being bought, and types 16, 26, and 47 being sold. The 甲 type, 16, was bought, and the retail sales also saw more buying than selling. Market prices across the board continued to rise by 0.2 or 0.3 yuan. Type 丁 for this month rose by 0.65 yuan. The floating sales of types 11 and 16 were particularly high. Apart from the 甲 type being supported by type 16 and not seeing highs or lows, the rest saw consistent small retreats of 0.05 to 0.1 to 0.3 yuan. The afternoon opening saw the sixteen type continuing to sell the aforementioned four types, and eleven and forty-three saw more buying. Therefore, although type 戊 fell by 0.25 to 0.4 yuan, types 乙 and 丙 rose by 0.1 or 0.2 yuan. Although 16 still saw buying, as 35 suddenly had a large number of longs being dropped and exiting, and the market lost 0.1 or 0.2 yuan, market prices were chaotic. Closing saw 16 once again focusing on pushing up the 甲 type, and the rest continued to see selling. Only 47 saw a bit of support. Therefore, aside from the 丁 type falling by 0.4 yuan, the rest continued to rise by 0.1 or 0.2 yuan. The overall market conditions were that the large player longs had no way out, so they thought of raising prices to avoid a sharp fall. But the environment didn't permit it, and it was only seen that their efforts were fruitless. Yesterday's result was that prices continued to rise by 0.2, 0.3, to 0.45 yuan. Only type 戊 this month had fallen back by 0.1 yuan. The total number of transactions was 3.945 million, of which type 丙 accounted for 1.665 million. The results of the rises and falls are compared in the table to the left (unit: yuan, trading unit: hundreds of yuan).

US Stock Market Rally Not Weak 179

Xinfeng Foreign Company reported that yesterday (the 2nd), US stocks, bonds, and commodities, excluding miscellaneous grains, tended to rise because of the continued expansion of domestic commerce. The US dollar rose slightly due to looser European cables, and buyers scrambled. As a result, industrial stocks were raised to a new high since 1931. The market then turned to railway stocks. The early market advanced under the leadership of automobile and steel stocks. Commercial stocks rose, and mail order, copper, oil, aircraft, and electrical appliances were particularly outstanding. Rubber stocks rose slightly, and agricultural implements loosened at the end. Steel and automobile stock longs also began unloading in the afternoon. Small exchange stocks rose slightly. In the bond market, domestic bonds and corporate bonds were very strong. The total daily turnover was 2.19 million shares. The Dow Jones New York Index is listed on the left.

According to market rumors, they were entrusted by a certain bank, and the mood grew increasingly nervous. However, trading of spot yarn felt increasingly sluggish. Broadly speaking, the market situation has not broken out of its hovering state.

Statistics on Chinese and Foreign Cotton Reserves — Wherein Each Package of Chinese Cotton Is Calculated at 500 Pounds — 181

Factories Buying Energetically - Hankou Cotton Market Particularly Active 182

(Hankou Correspondence) Cotton in the city is scarce due to the high prices in the producing areas. City reserves are less than 80,000 bales, and quite a few of these are in the hands of hoarders. As it is between harvests, they expect market prices to rise and are unwilling to sell. In addition, the cotton reserves of the Hankou yarn factories are extremely low. Along with the brisk sales of yarn, buying will inevitably rise. The yarn factories in Hunan and Jiujiang are taking the opportunity to buy, and Shanghai factories and speculators, seeing the rise in Shanghai cotton prices, are also buying in Hankou. Therefore, the market is active. Because hoarders are unwilling to sell, market prices have a tendency to continue to rise. Reserves surveyed in the middle of the month: 62,000 dan of fine staple cotton, 18,000 dan of coarse staple cotton. The price per 100 市斤 (a unit of weight): 41 yuan for superior grade fine staple cotton, 39 yuan for ordinary, 38 yuan for superior grade coarse staple cotton, 36 yuan for ordinary.

US Cotton Market Gradually Stabilizing 183

Yesterday's opening of the American cotton market saw traders and foreign companies buying and few sellers. New buyers appeared, and each month increased by 1 to 5 points. After careful research, some merchants believe that the proposed cotton lending program is constructive, as the lending limit is low, low prices can be avoided, and it does not compete with new cotton. Therefore, the market gradually stabilized. Afterwards, there was slight hedging and profit-taking, but the increased demand for July was absorbed. As a result, there were 13 points, and futures rose 9 to 13 points. British spot cotton fell by 3 points, and futures fell by 2 points. Indian cotton saw slight speculative buying, and recent short positions moved to far months. Calicut fell by 1 rupee, Oomra fell by 1.5 to 1.75 rupees, and Broach fell by 1.75 to 2.25 rupees. The original telegram is recorded to the left. (Telegram on the 2nd)

Also, according to the Bombay telegram, the opening forecast for Broach cotton for the March/April/May period was 198.5 rupees, up 1.75 rupees from the previous day's close, and the opening forecast for Broach for the July/August period was 200.5 rupees, up 1.75 rupees from the previous day's close.

Grains - Imported Rice and Foreign Wheat Slightly Weak 184

Yesterday in the imported rice market, continued arrivals from various ports in the Yangtze River and Wenzhou and Taizhou, but limited arrivals. Owners' thoughts remained tight. However, due to the approach of the Qingming Festival, local customers' sales were stagnant. Although small hoarders were active, trading was small, and some floating parties sought to sell. This market's appetite was also not as active as it had been a few days ago. Prices at each top-tier level uniformly trended weaker. Although the market was similar to the previous day, the actual value has been reduced by 2 or 3 分 (a unit of currency). However, if sales are strong after the festival, the market can turn around. Total daily openings: 1,670 packages of Jiangxi rice, 68 packages of Wuhu and Anqing, 600 packages of Jiangbei fire rice, 150 packages of Taizhou rice, and a shortage of 50 packages of broken rice.

There was spotty light rain in the southwest United States. Prices fell due to weakness in foreign markets and short-sellers unloading. Tang Mawen estimated the harvest of winter wheat at 530 million bushels, and Snow estimated it at 520 million bushels.

Thin indica rice fell by slightly more. Du Yangjian rice has not been traded, apart from Bian Yuan Ping rice trending weaker.

(North Shanghai) Yesterday, the weather was sunny and warm. There were 32 or 33 sources downriver. Store employees were mostly returning home to sweep graves, and trading was small. Soybean Oil Market Strong Like Yesterday 186

The soybean oil cake market was characterized by low spot arrivals and active sales, resulting in insufficient reserves. Furthermore, prices in the producing areas steadily increased, especially with frequent price rises communicated from Liaoning. The market was always optimistic. Yesterday, due to consecutive market holidays, local firms received telegrams from Dalian, noting that spot prices there were climbing intermittently. There were also numerous rumors in the market, with news spreading that a certain party was aggressively buying. As a result, market sentiment grew even firmer. Businesses and groups covering their positions were active. The afternoon saw even more dramatic gains, with the listed oil for April/May rising sharply by 0.65 yuan. The listed prices for other months also increased by 0.035 to 0.05 yuan, and listed soybean cake also increased by 0.03 to 0.04 yuan, while listed soybeans increased by 0.06 to 0.07 yuan.

The soybean oil cake market was in high spirits. The rally has not stopped. Although spot sales lacked large-scale purchases, the tendency remained strong due to the combined effects of environmental conditions and tight supplies. Yesterday's market recorded three train cars of Chen soybeans from Bengbu, 1,600 packages of border soybeans from Hankou, 300 packages of Du soybeans, 500 packages of Sha Huang soybeans, 29,500 pieces of soybean cake for both spot and future delivery, 720 pieces of soybean oil for both spot and future delivery, and 550 pieces of peanut oil.

Statistics on Rice, Wheat, Oil, Soybeans, Cake, Hemp, and Kernel (2) From March 21 to March 31

Oil Market - Sesame Oil Continues to Surge 187

Since sesame oil prices surged to 25.6 yuan last week, producing areas have also taken notice and prices have risen. As a result, the volume of goods arriving from various sources remains low. Coupled with the daily rise in raw material costs, owners' intention to sell has become firmer. It was reported that 340 or 350 cans of Huaiyuan goods had been opened previously, but the price increased to 27 yuan as a local business bought them, increasing sharply by 1.4 yuan. It is noted that there were approximately 30,000 cans of accumulated goods in the city. Although there were no large transactions, prices cannot be ignored due to the high price of raw materials.

Yesterday's sugar market was flat. Trading remained flat. 320 packages of Grade 5 Yang coarse white Guangdong goods were traded at 22.85 yuan, 100 packages of Shantou goods were traded at 21.65 yuan, and 60 packages of Grade 1 cotton white were traded at 20.9 yuan. Grade 2 cotton white and mid-level sand white sugars were not traded.

Dried and Preserved Goods - Jinshan Lychee Dries Gradually Becoming Scarce 189

Due to the thin harvest last year, the amount of Jinshan lychee dries arriving and in stock was low. Therefore, prices were very high. However, businesses in the industry predict that this year's harvest will increase. According to news from the producing areas, the seedlings have not sprouted due to the unresolved spring chill. Observations regarding the harvest are uncertain. Therefore, Shanghai has not seen much activity. Current stocks in the market are indeed limited, with only slightly more than 100 boxes of flat twigs and 400 or 500 boxes of round twigs. Traders are calling for 82 or 83 yuan for high-quality flat twigs and 70 yuan for high-quality round twigs, with lower prices for lower quality goods.

Textiles Domestic Woolen Fabrics Sales Increasingly Brisk 190

Domestic woolen fabrics have seen continued and broad sales recently. Zhanghua and Haijing have both released samples of Western-style suit materials. In recent years, all sectors have favored wearing domestic goods. Currently, popular and affordable woolen fabrics like serge and tweed in various men's and women's colors are selling well. Yihua's sales are particularly strong, followed by Zhanghua in second place, Haijing in third, and then Unified and Wuxi Xiejing. Hailin's thick serge, 918 serge, and various Huate tweeds are even more renowned, displaying a bold ambition to defeat imported goods. In the capital, sales of domestic woolen fabrics and knitwear have surged. Yesterday, Unified's No. 1 Western suit fabric sold for four yuan and thirty cents, No. 2 for three yuan and sixty cents. Xiejing's medium-thick serge was four yuan and twenty cents, checkered gabardine three yuan and fifty cents, and Zhanghua Jingqing fabric sold for one yuan and sixty cents.

Metals West Iron Sales Brisk Significant Arrivals of Big Guangdong Leather 191

West iron manufacturers have been expanding their business considerably in recent days, with dozens of transactions occurring daily. Customer support is also strong, leading to a particularly prosperous market trend. Prices are quite firm due to holders' insistence on high prices and scarce arrivals. Each box sells for thirty-five yuan, five jiao more than before. According to overseas pricing, the most recent price is seven yuan and five jiao in gold, and there are no spot goods arriving in Shanghai in the near future, so the market situation is quite optimistic.

The source of Big Guangdong leather has always been mostly British, American and German goods. Recently, however, Japan has also shipped a large quantity of spot goods. The market is softer than before, with each picul selling for eight yuan, two jiao and five fen (thick colorful), while thin colorful sells for nine yuan, four jiao and five fen per picul. Transactions are sluggish due to inactivity by customers, resulting in a rather stagnant market.

How to Get Rid of Bad Habits? 193

— Lan Shan

Dear children, today I am here to talk to you about the problem of habits.

In our daily life, diet, actions, and speech, everyone has some habits; if these habits are good, then their life is also good; if their habits are irregular, then their life is also irregular. For example, someone who is in the habit of getting up early, loving cleanliness, studying diligently, abstaining from snacks, and saving money, do you think this is a good life habit? Who wouldn't like a child who has these good life habits? Being a good student at school and a good child at home is the most honorable thing, and these glorious honors all come from having good life habits.

For example, among your classmates, there is a child who is always late for the first class because he gets up late, so will the teacher and classmates praise him? Every time he is unable to recite or write from memory because he is unwilling to study diligently, do you want to make fun of him? Also, because he doesn't know how to be clean, he often gets a large patch of ink on his face and shirt, and wipes clumps of snot on his sleeves, do you find him disgusting? If he doesn't know how to treat people kindly and often scolds his classmates for small things, do you like him? I think you probably won't like such a detestable person, will you? Do you know why he is not liked by you? This is because bad life habits have harmed him, because he has not developed good habits!

Dear children, after seeing the two examples I mentioned above, everyone must have a good understanding in their hearts. Now I will say a little more, that is, habits are not innate, but are learned one by one. Habits are formed in childhood, so in childhood, you must be careful about all your actions, and always ask yourself: "Is what I am doing good? Or is it bad?" If you feel it is bad, you must correct it immediately and not be sloppy. If you are sloppy, it will become a bad habit in the future, and it will be very difficult to change at that time.

Good children, they will often examine themselves and will not be harmed by bad habits.

How to Study Science? 194

— Yue Qi

To be a person in the modern world, one should have some basic knowledge of various sciences; and the first step in studying various sciences must start from childhood.

Some people say: Children's minds are simple, so children are not easy to learn science.

Precisely because children's minds are simple, children are easier to approach science than adults. Science is nothing more than the study of the conditions under which special events occur. From a child's simple mind, everything is special and enough to arouse his curiosity and desire for knowledge. The sun, moon, stars, thunder, lightning, wind, and rain, as well as everyday events such as water boiling in a pot placed on the fire and a stone falling down, are generally considered obvious and unquestionable events by sophisticated adults, but for innocent children, there is always the question of "how it happens." Doubt is the only important condition for studying science; children who are good at doubting are of course more likely to learn science naturally than adults. There are many opportunities for children to acquire scientific knowledge. How to use these opportunities to instill scientific knowledge into children is the responsibility of adults who are responsible for educating children.

Some people also say: Science is dry and boring, not liked by children's nature.

This statement is even more wrong. As long as the teaching is proper, science is not only often interesting but also has the beautiful fairyland in fairy tales that children's nature likes.

"Sleeping Beauty in the Woods" is one of the fairy tales that children love to hear. In this story, the fairy used her magic in a fit of anger. As a result, the princess in the palace, the horses in the stable, the dogs in the courtyard, the pigeons on the roof, the cooks in the kitchen, and all the courtiers of the emperor and empress were put to sleep by her magic. A dense fence grew around the palace, and the interior of the palace became as silent as death. It wasn't until a brave prince came a hundred years later that the fence of thorns, wearing bright floral clothes, unraveled before him; the prince entered the palace and went to the room where the princess was sleeping soundly, and a sweet kiss instantly revived her and the people around her.

Are there similar fairy tales in science? Yes. Water is a very busy and very active thing in the world. It either flows in the river, or rushes against the rocks, or splashes from the fountain, or drips from the roof, and when the wind blows on the surface of the pond, it wrinkles into whirlpools. However, this busy and active water can sometimes suddenly be enchanted and become completely still. On a cold winter morning, looking out the window, the river that was still flowing next to the house yesterday is now still, and the rocks that were washed by the river are surrounded by hard ice. The ripples on the pond have stopped moving. The water droplets dripping from the roof have become transparent icicles. Every tree has crystal-like water droplets dozing there. The fountain has become a glass tree, hanging upside down with many transparent, long, pointed leaves. It turns out that they have all been enchanted by the "Ice Fairy," who holds "ice" tightly, not letting it slip away.

After a few weeks, maybe a few days, maybe only a few hours, the brave sun shines on the earth. The gray clouds dissipated before him, just like the fence in the story unraveled before the prince: the sunlight and the frozen water gave a gentle kiss, and it melted, just like the prince's sweet kiss revived the princess. So the river flowed again, the water droplets dripped again, the fountain splashed again, and everything returned to life under the bright and warm sunlight.

In science, there are countless beautiful and moving stories like fairy tales. Who says science is dry and boring?

The field of science is infinite, and the life of a person is limited. Children who aspire to study science must not miss the opportunity to learn early!

How to Improve Your Writing? 195

— Liu Sijun

Children: In your Chinese language class at school, the subject with the fewest points is probably writing. You may think that writing is difficult, but it is not. Here are some ways to tell you how to improve your writing.

People in the past have long said that to be good at Chinese and write well, you should read, read, and write more, but there is still room for discussion on how to read, read, and write more.

What should you read more? I think that to improve your writing, you should not only read Chinese, but you should read all kinds of books. why? Because writing represents language, and you must know something before you can speak it, so you must also know something before you can write it. To know something, you must read all kinds of books. Reading only Chinese will limit what you know.

The method of reading more should be to read more Chinese books. Because reading more is to seek more knowledge, the scope should be wide. Reading more is not only to seek knowledge, but also to study its structure, sentence structure, and rhetoric. In other words: it is not only to seek its content, but also to study its form; that is, words. Chinese books are more particular about literature, so reading more is limited to Chinese.

In addition to writing in school, you should also practice writing automatically. It is better to write diaries than to write many long articles automatically. why? Because at this time, your knowledge is not wide, and your thoughts are immature, so you will feel difficult to write. Diaries are not limited by topics, regardless of length. As long as you have some feelings or trivia, you can write. Therefore, writing diaries is the best way to practice writing.

In addition, to improve writing, you must also practice two things: one is observation, and the other is thinking. Observation allows you to increase your knowledge; thinking allows you to train your thinking. Both are indispensable elements for improving writing.

How to Choose Story Books? 196

— Zhu Ying

The story books currently popular in the market generally fall into the following three types: Mythical stories, Famous people stories, Science stories.

Mythical stories are divided into two types: one is issued by formal bookstores, which are all stories about wind old men, snow girls, monkey brothers, white rabbit sisters, as well as moon palace fairylands, and island gods. There is also a kind that is printed by informal bookstores? and sold by door-panel book stalls, such as sword fairies, knights, fox spirits, and monsters.

Among the stories of famous people, there are famous people from China and foreign countries, ancient and modern, such as politicians, scientists, explorers, loyal ministers, filial sons, and martyrs. But at the same time, there are also many that are compiled with the traditional feudal ideology of China as the center.

Because science stories are children's reading materials, many of them deliberately make scientific principles overly magical in order to arouse children's reading interest. But there are naturally very reasonable ones.

Recently, according to a friend who works in the book industry, "Mythical stories sell the best, followed by stories of famous people, but only 15% of the sales of mythical stories. Science stories, except for those that are too magical, almost like magic, can occasionally sell a few copies. Reasonable science stories are simply not asked about. After publication, there is no possibility of reprinting."

Then, I met a friend who was a primary school principal and talked to him about the problem of primary school students reading stories. He said, "Primary school students in the early grades love to read stories such as wind old men and snow girls. High school students love to read sword fairies and knights. This is almost a common phenomenon in the primary school student world. Stories of famous people and science stories are forced upon high school students, but they seem to have no interest at all, and they are not as interesting as reading mythical stories."

Why are meaningless mythical stories so popular, and more valuable stories, such as stories of famous people and science stories, unpopular with children?

Although this is a small problem, I think this is quite serious for the future of children, so I specially put it forward and ask educators to find ways to correct it.

How to Organize a "Reading Friendship Association"? 197

— Zeng Geng

Dear children, after your classes, when you are on Sundays or holidays, don't you feel the monotony and boredom of reading alone? I know that you have also lost interest in self-study alone, and you have also encountered difficulties in understanding the books because of reading alone. Now I would like to launch a "Children's Reading Friendship Association" to help you solve difficulties and to adjust your monotony.

This "Children's Reading Friendship Association" can be established with two or more people. We don't need to collect membership fees, etc. As long as everyone takes out their own books, chooses a relatively quiet place, and everyone reads, reads, writes, and does the homework that the teacher asks us to do outside of class together. If there are places that we don't understand, we research and discuss them with each other. If we encounter problems that cannot be solved, we can temporarily retain them and ask our parents and teachers for guidance.

In addition to the mutual discussion of reading, we also need to seek cooperation in labor, and we also need to seek contact in friendship. A small group is a microcosm of society. If you get used to the collective life of the group, then you will not feel strange when you step into society in the future.

Here, let me put the charter of the "Children's Reading Friendship Association" below:

1. Name - Children's Reading Friendship Association.

2. Purpose - The purpose is to discuss knowledge, connect feelings, and develop the habit of group life.

3. Members - If the character is upright and those who are determined to study, they can be members of this association.

4. Organization The association has one president, who is responsible for convening, and two executives, who are responsible for the arrangement of the association.

5. Instructor - The association may hire one parent and teacher as instructors, who are responsible for teaching.

Dear children, after reading the above five very simple articles of association, I think it is definitely not a very difficult thing, right? I hope that in the future, you will invite a few classmates or neighboring children to prepare together and organize a very sound "Children's Reading Friendship Association" to work hard on the discussion of your knowledge, the connection of feelings, and the development of group life habits.

The Big-Bellied Snake Lied 204

— Xie Jiting, student of Shanghai Minsheng Primary School

There was a farmer who, when he came back from planting his fields, walked across a ditch and saw a big-bellied female snake trying to cross the ditch but couldn't get over it. He used a hoe to help it over. The female snake returned to the cave and said to the male snake, "I just encountered danger and almost lost my life." The male snake said, "How could you almost lose your life?" The female snake said, "When I was crossing the ditch, a farmer wanted to hit me with a hoe. Fortunately, I escaped quickly, otherwise I would have been killed by him." The male snake said, "I will definitely avenge you tonight."

In the evening, he found the farmer's house and lay on the roof of the farmer's bed, waiting for an opportunity. Coincidentally, the farmer's wife was also big-bellied. When she went to bed, she couldn't climb up, so the farmer helped her up to the bed. The farmer also told his wife in detail about helping the big-bellied snake cross the ditch on the road. The male snake heard this on the roof and knew that the female snake was lying. He was very angry. He returned to the cave and bit the female snake to death.

Do Not Spit Anywhere 205

— Xu Meixian, student of Shanghai Qinghua Primary School

There is a very strict school rule in our school: "That is, no spitting anywhere." The teacher told us: "Sputum is the most unclean thing, it contains bacteria. If the sputum of a patient is dried by the wind, the bacteria will fly with the air and be inhaled into people's mouths and noses, reaching the lungs." Therefore, sputum is a medium for infectious diseases, and having the habit of spitting often makes people disgusted. One day a student forgot this school rule and with a whoosh, spat a mouthful of sputum on the ground. In this situation, I think it is best to punish him to sweep the floor for a week and pour the spittoon for a week, so that they can be taught this lesson and can repent of their past mistakes and spit the sputum into the spittoon. If you don't see the spittoon, everyone should prepare a piece of paper. In this way! If everyone does this, from now on, they will develop good habits.

Respectfully Announcing to the Nation's Children 217

— Jian Ping

Children's Day is here, and as usual, there's a burst of enthusiasm. Adults and teachers are also excitedly holding meetings, performing rituals, and expanding celebrations. But, if an tactless person asks: What good does this do for the children? Only heaven knows. Let's put that aside for now and talk about the miracle of this brave "West Lake Children's Travel Group" as a tribute to Children's Day.

Readers probably won't forget. On March 29th, ten elementary school students from Wengjia Hill Elementary School in Hangzhou came to meet with people in Shanghai at the South Railway Station. What's strange is that they are all underage children, the oldest being a fifteen-year-old girl. They don't want adult leaders; they are completely self-organized. Their purpose is because they "don't want to be trapped forever in cage-like schools or isolated mountain villages," and they "want to use the vast society as a school, and the vast masses as teachers. They want to enter all kinds of different societies, experience all kinds of different lives, contact all kinds of different people, and learn all kinds of different knowledge," so they came to Shanghai. Their expenses also come from the manuscript fees earned from writing little teacher's diaries, and they only brought eighty dollars, which they were afraid would not be enough, so they also brought a book they wrote themselves, "Experiences in Popularizing Education," which they planned to sell to exchange for travel expenses. At the same time, their greater reason is to test whether they have the ability to govern themselves away from their parents' families and schools; and their purpose in coming to Shanghai is not for the bustling traffic and extravagant luxury here, but to see the suffering of people in all walks of life, and to what extent they are invaded and oppressed. These days they are realizing their ideals, visiting various places, and maybe they will return to school on April 5th. What kind of feelings will we have about such a tour group? Especially a group of children's experts.

On March 30th, they also issued a "Respectfully Announcing to the Nation's Children," but we haven't seen that declaration published in the newspaper yet, but even if we don't read that declaration, we can understand the power of that declaration, because their own "actions" are the most powerful "Respectfully Announcing to the Nation's Children." This "declaration" written with "facts" not only teaches the nation's dazed wealthy children, and the bookish elementary school students who don't understand things, but also honestly teaches the general so-called children's education experts who are working hard on theory and completely failing to actually consider children. It has opened up a bright road for China's children.

Finally, we reiterate the significance of this living "Respectfully Announcing to the Nation's Children" and propose a motion to Children's Day: in such a critical moment of national crisis, even elementary school students should not bury their heads in textbooks in the classroom. He wants to read living books, to read books with society as a textbook. At the same time, the children's education we need is children's education that matches Weng's extraordinary period of national disaster, cultivating children's correct understanding of society and fully developing children's abilities; rather than general bureaucratic aristocratic education. Teachers who want to seek happiness for children, please be thorough! Don't put effort into novel patterns anymore.

Two Mothers and Daughters 218

— Lin Na

Because I had to move out of a fellow villager's shop, I went to Buried Street to find a house. This street is in a barren area, which the Manila people call a slum. It's a路 , filled with garbage, dust, and bare-headed, barefooted dirty children all year round. There are only four or five pitiful "vegetable shops" from the beginning to the end of the street, and quarrels and fights are common.

After turning over Buried Bridge, I slowed down and walked slowly, paying attention to the shops on both sides: to see if there were any houses with signs for rent. Finally, at the end of the street, I found one with a crookedly written sign on the door: Room to Let. So I ran around this house to see if there was anything, and then ran to the door and knocked. After four or five minutes, I heard a broken voice yelling from inside, and then the door opened with an "ah." It was an old woman with a limp and crutches. I explained my purpose, and she looked me up and down, then invited me in.

Although she was an old woman with a limp, she climbed the stairs very quickly, not at all like someone with a disease. She chattered as she climbed the corroded stairs, sighing as she said:

Our house, sir, I guarantee you will be satisfied at first sight, the light and air are something you can't find anywhere in Buried Street. As for the residents, there's only our family, a mother and daughter, no children to disturb you. ..., she led me to stand outside a room, gently tapping the floor with her crutch, and warmly called to the front厢房: Tierra! A guest has come to see the house, quickly bring out the key.

A crisp voice from the front厢房 answered, followed by a delicate sound of slippers, and a fifteen or sixteen-year-old girl ran out half-naked. She nodded slightly to me, and I hurriedly nodded back, feeling a little warm on my face.

The house was looked at, now it was our turn to talk about the price, they asked for five pesos a month as soon as they opened their mouths, I said; "Damn! What kind of street is this, what kind of house is this, five pesos a month". The old woman became anxious, and heavily tapped her crutch, and said in a hoarse voice: "Sir, you have to see clearly! This has good air, good light, and we don't have children, just a clean mother and daughter." ...

I continued: "Old lady, I already knew that a long time ago, but the rent is a bit too expensive, I can't afford it"! So I prepared to pick up my hat, say sorry, and run away. The old woman anxiously stood up and hurriedly held down my hat, and directly reduced the rent to three and a half pesos. I thought it was about right, so I agreed, put down a deposit of one peso, said I would move in that night, and left.

That night, I hired a horse carriage, and moved in a box of books, two pieces of broken luggage, and a bundle of quilts, and a brand new independent life began.

After a few days, the livelihood issues of these two lonely mothers and daughters gradually attracted my attention, and I quickly became interested in them. That失誤 six-year-old girl sat at home all day, accompanied by the limping old woman. During the day, when I got tired of reading in the back pavilion, I would often sit quietly and listen to the laughter coming from the front厢房. I savored and researched its meaning. This laughter was particularly loud sometimes coming from the broken voice of that limping old woman, and was sometimes mixed with the sound of tapping crutches and stomping feet, which clearly indicated that something funny was making her dance with joy.

After a burst of laughter, I could clearly hear the good girl's voice again, she said loudly, in a serious posture: "... so Paul began his heroic voyage. This voyage took a lot of his hard work, because God, in order to test whether he had unwavering faith, sent many gods who wielded thunder, rain, wind, and electricity, causing the sea island's wind and waves to rage: but Paul was not afraid at all, he resolutely and heroically steered the boat and advanced through the raging waves. Finally, the coral island was discovered, and he suddenly became the richest man in the world. ..."

This narration of the adventure story moved the limping old woman. Because her diseased foot, her crutch, no longer tapped loudly on the floor. I believe she must have yearned for that beautiful coral island.

When I went out for dinner in the evening, the front厢房 was already quiet. I could no longer hear the limping old woman's broken laughter, or Tierra's narration of adventure stories. Only a heavy silence. Tierra was gone, and the old woman sat blankly on a broken sofa, her face buried in her arms. Perhaps the excessive loneliness made her feel depressed, so every time she heard my footsteps, she would come limping out of the front厢房 with her crutch, and道 to me. But when I asked her if she had had dinner, her face would slightly flush, and she would shake her head shamefully, saying "Tierra has already gone out to buy it..."

Often, not long after, the sound of footsteps on the扶梯响了, which meant that Tierra had already returned: but not only her alone, but also another person. This person, who was brought from the street corner or somewhere, was sometimes a drunken American sailor, sometimes a stingy coachman, and sometimes a laborer. But the old woman would often pretend not to know, when I first moved in, I didn't know what was going on and often told her: "Tierra has already returned"! She would deliberately change the subject, and entangle me with various questions, preventing me from focusing on listening to the vulgar conversations, laughter, and various unpleasant sounds that could be heard in the front厢房 at this time. Sometimes she would argue with me about the existence of God, and sometimes she would question me: Do the Japanese have any ambitions for the Philippines? This old woman was cultured, and it is said that she used to come from a wealthy family, but later fell into decline.

When our discussions sometimes stopped, I could clearly hear the various movements and sounds in the front厢房. Sometimes it was Tierra's weak complaints and sobs, sometimes it was panting and obscene浪语. At this time, the old woman was silent, her heart torn by sorrow.

Finally, these thugs were sent away, and Tierra followed them out after a while: but she returned quickly, gently knocking on our door, and said in a criminal and timid voice: Mom, the bread is bought!

The old woman hurriedly replied gently, and turned back to me apologetically: I'm sorry, sir, there was a lot of noise tonight.... She also said good night before quietly, like a persecuted mouse, limping out.

Tokyo Miscellany 219

— Lei Shi Yu

Tea, Saloons, Coffee

If you happen to walk into any street and your ears are directly catching the sound waves of a phonograph flowing out from a window or a half-open door, friend, if you don't have urgent business to attend to, or if you have that kind of interesting feeling, then, please slow down your pace, (even just for a moment is fine), turn your head and glance at the sign on the door or the corner of the door frame, like a guardhouse sentry, to see if there are words like "tea" or "pure tea." No, even someone who has just arrived in Tokyo wouldn't be so dull-witted as to stand there staring; aren't those words visible from afar? Moreover, the Western-style facade already displays a distinctive mark. So, to put it bluntly, if you're happy to, please go in and rest for a while. As you are about to walk in, a young tea girl, with a charming smile, either leaning by the door or "rushing up" to greet you, calls out in a soft, elastic, and clear tone:

——Irasshai! (Welcome!)

Inside, there are simple and elegant tables arranged, and if you want something more refined, there are also sofas for you to sit on. Drink whatever you like; there's black tea, coffee, lemon, etc. You don't have to be pretentious or act like a big shot; drink a cup of whatever for a dime or fifteen cents, and sit for an hour or two if you like. There is various music to cleanse your ears, and of course, there are newspapers for you to browse. You don't have to listen or look, and no one will laugh if you just sit there alone. If you feel lonely, you can invite a friend or two, or chat with a familiar tea girl. Because those customers are just students, scholars, or people of leisure, they won't cause any disturbance, so you can sit down with peace of mind.

I heard that during the period around the October Revolution, Russian poets often read poetry or discussed issues in tea shops.

But the tea shops in Tokyo, at least, serve the function of providing leisure for the petty bourgeoisie in general.

If you encounter a place that is similar in style, but with a more extravagant facade, a larger scale, and signs marked: Cafe or "Western Liquor," then you should at least first assess the savings in your pocket before entering. When you go in, don't be too pretentious, nor too flashy; if you're too pretentious, the coffeehouse intellectuals will ridicule you as if you were a fool; if you act too much like a big spender, you will lose the feeling of thrift in the embrace and chattering voices of the girls. Even if you are in a normal pose, you should also prepare to deal with the demands of the girls who come to sit with you or sit opposite you, almost in rotation, asking "I want a cup of something" or "Please give me a little something" when they leave.

It is the abject life that devours their sense of shame and hones their cunning skills.

People who go to coffee shops are considered qualified only if they can satisfy all or part of their desires.

"Western Liquor" is about the same, or perhaps even more intoxicating, because the power of "liquor" seems stronger than the power of "coffee." Although various kinds of wine are also drunk in coffee shops. However, I don't like alcohol, and my experience in that area is very insufficient; I only remember having seen colorful clothes, bright red lips, and peach-like cheeks once or twice...
